abhivādayiṃ   ApBud Yāvatā Buddhakhettesu ratanā vijjanti saṅkhiyā  ākāsaṭṭhā ca bhūmaṭṭhā manasā sabbam āhare  ApBud Tattha rūpiyabhūmiyaṃ pāsādaṃ māpaye ahaṃ  nekabhūmiṃ ratanamayaṃ ubbiddhaṃ nabham uggataṃ   ApBud Vicittathambhaṃ sukataṃ suvibhattaṃ mahārahaṃ  kanakāmayasaṅghātaṃ toraṇacchattamaṇḍitaṃ  ApBud Paṭhamā veluriyā bhūmi vimalabbhasamā subhā  naḷinājalajākiṇṇā varakañcanabhūmiyā   ApBud Pavāḷaṃ sapavāḷavaṇṇā kācilohitakāsubhā  indagopakavaṇṇābhā bhūmi obhāsati disā   ApBud Suvibhattā gharamukhā niyyuhā sīhapañjarā  caturo vedikā jālā gandhaveḷā manoramā   ApBud Nīlā pītā Buddhāpadānaṃ                        Ratanagabbhaṃ pavisitvā kesarī va guhāsayā  mahārahamhi sayane sīhaseyyam akappayuṃ   ApBud Sampajānā samuṭṭhāya sayane pallaṅkam ābhujuṃ gocaraṃ sabbabuddhānaṃ jhānaratisamappitā   ApBud Aññe dhammāni desenti aññe kīḷanti iddhiyā  aññe abhiññā appenti abhiññāvasibhāvitā  vikubbanā vikubbanti aññe nekasatasahassiyo   ApBud Buddhā pi buddhe pucchanti visayaṃ ca sāvakā paricārakā  evaṃ ratīsu rammānā pāsāde bhiramanti te   ApBud Suvaṇṇajālābhi saṃyuttaṃ rajatajālamaṇīhi ca  muttajālaparikkhittaṃ chattaṃ dhārentu matthake   ApBud Bhavantu celavitānā ravantu tā  sabbā saṅgītī vattantu pāsādassa sāmantato   ApBud                            ApadānaYāvatā buddhakhettamhi cakkavāle camuppari  mahantā jotisampannā acchiddā ratanāmayā   ApBud Tiṭṭhantu dinnaṃ puññaphalaṃ mayā  ye ca tattha na jānanti devā gantvā nivedayuṃ  ApBud Sabbe lokamhi ye sattā jīvantāhārahetukā  manuññaṃ bhojanaṃ sabbaṃ labhantu mama cetasā   ApBud Manasā dānaṃ mayā dinnaṃ manasā pasādam āvahiṃ pūjitā sabbaSambuddhā paccekā jinasāvakā   ApBud Tena kammena sukatena cetanā paṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsam agañch ahaṃ   ApBud Duve bhave pajānāmi devatte atha mānuse  aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi manasā patthanāphalaṃ   ApBud Devānaṃ adhiko homi bhavāmi manujādhipo  rūpalakkhaṇasampanno paññāya asamo bhave   ApBud Bhojanaṃ vividhaṃ seṭṭhaṃ ratanañ ca anappakaṃ ca vimānane  sabbattha samako hutvā patto sambodhim uttamaṃ   ApBud Kosajjaṃ bhayato disvā viriyañ cāpi khemato  āraddhavīriyā hotha esā Buddhānusāsanī   ApBud Vivādaṃ bhayato disvā avivādaṃ ca sambhāvayamāno Buddhānaṃ padāniyaṃ nāma dhammapariyāyaṃ abhāsitthā tiBuddhāpadānaṃ samattaṃIIPACCEKABUDDHĀPADĀNAṂAtha paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ suṇāthaTathāgataṃ Jetavane vasantaṃ apucchi Vedehamuni nataṅgo  ‘Paccekabuddhā kira nāma honti bhavanti te hetuhi kehi dhīrā   ApPac Tadāha sabbaññuvaro mahesi Ānandabhaddaṃ madhurassarena  Ye sabbabuddhesu katādhikārā aladdhamokkhā Jinasāsanesu   ApPac Ten eva saṃvegamukhena dhīrā vināpi buddhehi sutikkhapaññā  ārammaṇenāpi parittakena paccekabodhiṃ anupāpuṇanti   ApPac Sabbamhi lokamhi mamaṃ ṭhapetvā paccekabuddhehi samo va n atthi  Tesaṃ imaṃ vaṇṇapadesamattaṃ vakkhām ahaṃ sādhu mahāmunīnaṃ   ApPac Sayaṃ eva buddhānaṃ mahāisīnaṃ sādhūni vākyāni madhuñ ca khuddaṃ  anuttaraṃ bhesajaṃ patthayantā suṇotha sabbe supasannacittā   ApPac Paccekabuddhānaṃ samāgatānaṃ paramparavyākaraṇāni yāni  ādīnavo yañ ca virāgavatthuṃ yathā ca bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu   ApPac                        ApadānaSaṃrāgavatthūsu virāgasaññī rattamhi lokamhi virattacittā  hitvā papañcaṃ jitaphanditāni tatth eva bodhiṃ anupāpuṇiṃsu   ApPac Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññataram pi tesaṃ  mettena cittena hitānukampī eko care khaggavisānakappo   ApPac Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ aviheṭhayaṃ aññataraṃ pi tesaṃ  na puttam iccheyya kuto sahāyaṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Saṃsaggajātassa bhavanti snehā snehanvayaṃ dukkhaṃ idaṃ pahoti  ādīnavaṃ snehajaṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Mitte suhajje anukampamāno hāpeti atthaṃ paṭibandhacitto  etaṃ bhayaṃ santhave pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Vaṃso visālo va yathā visatto puttesu dāresu ca yā apekkhā  vaṃsakkaḷīro va asajjamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Migo araññamhi yathā abandho yenicchakaṃ gacchati gocarāya  viññu naro seritaṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Āmantaṇā hoti sahāyamajjhe vāse ṭhāne gamane cārikāya  anabhijjhitaṃ seritaṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Khiḍḍā ratī hoti sahāyamajjhe puttesu pemaṃ vipulañ ca hoti  piyavippayogaṃ vijigucchamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ                  Catuddiso appaṭigho ca hoti santussamāno itarītarena  parissayānaṃ sahitā achambhī eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Dussaṅgahā pabbajitā pi eke atho gahaṭṭhā gharam āvasantā  apposukko paraputtesu hutvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Oropayitvā gihibyañjanāni sañchinnapatto yathā koviḷāro  chetvāna vīro gihibandhanāni eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhīraṃ  abhibhūya sabbāni parissayāni careyya ten attamano satīmā   ApPac No ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāri dhīraṃ  rājā va raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya eko care mātaṅgaraññe va nāgo   ApPac addhā pasaṃsāma sahāyasampadaṃ seṭṭhā samā sevitabbā sahāyā  ete aladdhā anavajjabhojī eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Disvā suvaṇṇassa pabhassarāni kammāraputtena suniṭṭhitāni  saṅghaṭṭamānāni duve bhujasmiṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Evaṃ dutiyena sahā mam assa vācābhilāpo abhisajjanā vā  etaṃ bhayaṃ āyatiṃ pekkhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac                       ApadānaKāmā hi citrā madhurā manoramā virūparūpena ApPac Sītañ ca uṇhañ ca khudaṃ pipāsaṃ vātātape daṃsasiriṃsape cā  sabbāni p etāni abhibhavitvā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Nāgo va yūthāni vivajjayitvā sañjātakhandho padumī uḷāro Diṭṭhīvisūkāni upātivatto patto niyāmaṃ paṭiladdhamaggo  uppannañāṇo mhi anaññaneyyo eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Nillolupo nikkuho nippipāso nimmakkho niddhantakasāvamoho  nirāsayo sabbaloke ApadānaVipiṭṭhikatvāna sukhaṃ dukkhañ ca pubbe va somanassaṃ domanassaṃ laddhān upekkhaṃ samathaṃ visuddhaṃ eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Āraddhaviriyo paramatthapattiyā alīnacitto akusītavutti  daḷhanikkamo thāmabalūpapanno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Paṭisallānajhānaṃ ariñcamāno dhammesu niccaṃ anudhammacārī  ādīnavaṃ sammasitā bhavesu eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Taṇhakkhayaṃ patthayaṃ appamatto anelamūgo sutavā satīmā  saṅkhātadhammo niyato padhānavā eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Sīho va saddesu asantasanto vāto va jālamhi asajjamāno  padumaṃ va toyena alimpamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Sīho yathā dāṭhabalī pasayha rājā migānaṃ abhibhuyyacārī  sevetha pantāni senāsanāni eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Mettam upekkhaṃ karuṇaṃ vimuttiṃ āsevamāno muditañ ca kāle  sabbena lokena avirujjhamāno eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Rāgañ ca dosañ ca pahāya mohaṃ sandālayitvāna saṃyojanāni  asantasaṃ jīvitasaṅkhayamhi eko care khaggavisāṇakappo   ApPac Paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ              Bhajanti sevanti ca kāraṇatthā nikkāraṇā dullabhā ajja mittā  attaṭṭhapaññā asucī manussā eko care khaggavisānakappo   ApPac Visuddhasīlā suvisuddhapaññā samāhitā jāgariyānuyuttā  vipassakā dhammavisesadassī maggaṅgabojjhaṅgagate vijaññā   ApPac Puññappaṇidhiñ ca tathānimittaṃ āsevayitvā Jinasāsanamhi  ye sāvakattaṃ na vajanti dhīrā bhavanti paccekajinā sayambhū   ApPac Mahantadhammā bahudhammakāyā cittissarā sabbadukkhoghatiṇṇā  udaggacittā paramatthadassī sīhopamā khaggavisāṇakappā   ApPac Santindriyā santamānā samādhī paccanta sattesu satippacārā  dīpā parattha idha vijjalantā paccekabuddhā satataṃ hitā me   ApPac Pahīnasabbāvaraṇā janindā lokappadīpā ghanakañcanābhā  nisaṃsayaṃ lokasudakkhiṇeyyā paccekabuddhā satataṃ hitā me   ApPac Paccekabuddhānaṃ subhāsitāni caranti lokamhi sadevakamhi  sutvā tathā ye na karonti bālā bhamanti dukkhesu punappunan te   ApPac Paccekabuddhānaṃ subhāsitāni madhuṃ yathā khuddam iva ssavantaṃ sutvā tathā ye paṭipattiyuttā bhavanti te saccadasā sapaññā  ApPac                       ApadānaPaccekabuddhehi Jinehi vuttā gāthā uḷārā abhinikkhamitvā  tā Sakyasīhena naruttamena pakāsitā dhammavijānanatthaṃ   ApPac Lokānukampāya imāni tesaṃ paccekabuddhānaṃ vikubbitāni  saṃvegasaṅgāmativaḍḍhanatthaṃ sayambhusīhena pakāsitāni ti   ApPac Paccekabuddhāpadānaṃ samattaṃ dutiyaṃIIITHERĀPADĀNAṂAtha therāpadānaṃ sunāthaHimavantass avidūre Lambako nāma pabbato  assamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā   ApTha Uttānakūlā nadikā supatiṭṭhā manoramā  sasuddhapuḷinākiṇṇā avidūre mam assamaṃ  ApTha Asakkharā apabbhārā sādu appaṭigandhikā  sandati nadikā tattha sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Kumbhīlā makarā c ettha suṃsumārā ca kacchapā  sandati nadikā tattha sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā jalajā muñjarohitā  vagguḷā ca patāyanti sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Ubho kūlesu nadiyā pupphino phalino dumā  ubhato abhilambanti sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Ambā kolakā tilakā pāṭalī sindhuvāritā  dibbā gandhā sampavanti pupphitā mama assame   ApTha Campakā saḷalā nīpā nāgapunnāgaketakā  dibbā gandhā sampavanti pupphitā mama assame   ApTha Atimuttā asokā ca bhaginimālā ca pupphitā  aṅkolā bimbijālā ca pupphitā mama assame   ApTha                       TherāpadānaKetakā kandalī c eva kebukā tiṇasūlikā  dibbā gandhā sampavanti sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Kaṇṇikārā kaṇikā ca asanā añjanī bahū  dibbā gandhā sampavanti sobhamānā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Punnāgā giripunnāgā koviḷārā ca pupphitā  dibbā gandhā sampavanti sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Uddālakā ca kuṭajā kadambā vakuḷā bahū  dibbā gandhā sampavanti sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha Āḷakā isimuggā ca kadalī mātuluṅgiyo  gandhodakena saṃvaddhā phalāni dhārayanti te   ApTha Aññe pupphanti padumā aññe jāyanti kesarī  aññe opupphā padumā taḷāke pupphitā tadā  ApTha Gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā niddhāvanti muḷāliyo  siṅghāṭipattamākiṇṇā sobhayanti taḷākaṃ tadā  ApTha Nayitā ambagandhī ca utūḷhi bandhujīvakā  dibbā gandhā sampavanti taḷāke pupphitā tadā   ApTha Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā valajā muñjarohitā  saṅkulā maggurā c eva vasanti taḷāke tadā   ApTha Kumbhīlā suṃsumārā ca tantiggāhā ca rakkhasā  ogahā ajagārā ca vasanti taḷake tadā   ApTha Pārevatā ravihaṃsā cakkavākā nadīcarā  kokilā sukasāḷī ca upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Kukutthakā kulīrakā vane pokkharasātakā  diṇḍibhā suvapotā ca upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha  Sāriputta                            Haṃsā koñcā mayūrā ca kokilā tambacūḷakā  sampakā jīvajīvā ca upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Kosikā poṭṭhasīsā ca kurarā senakā bahū  mahākāḷā ca sakuṇā upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Pasadā ca varāhā ca vakabheraṇḍakā bahū  rohiccā suggapotā ca upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Sīhā vyagghā ca dīpī ca acchakokataracchayo  tidhappabhinnā mātaṅgā upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Kinnarā vānarā c eva atho pi vanakammikā  cetā ca luddakā c eva upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Tiṇḍukāni piyālāni madhuke kāsumāriyo  dhuvaphalāni dhārenti avidūre mam assamaṃ   ApTha Kosumbhā saḷalā nīpā sāraphalasamāyutā  dhuvaṃ phalāni dhārenti avidūre mam assamaṃ   ApTha Harīṭakā āmalakā ambā jambuvibhīṭakā  kolā bhallātakā bellā phalāni dhārayanti te   ApTha Ālulā ca kalambā ca bilāni takkaḷāni ca  jīvakā sahakā c eva bahukā mama assame   ApTha Assamassāvidūramhi taḷākā susunimmitā  acchodakā sitajalā supatitthā manoramā   ApTha Padumuppalasañchannā puṇḍarīkasamāyutā  mandālakehi sañchannā dibbo gandho pavāyati   ApTha Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampanne pupphite phalite vane  sukate assame ramme viharāmi ahaṃ tadā  ApTha Sīlavā vatasampanno jhāyī jhānarato sadā  pañcābhiññāphalappatto Surucī nāma tāpaso   ApTha Catubbīsasahassāni sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ  sabbe ca brāhmaṇā ete jātimanto yasassino   ApTha Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca sanighaṇḍu sakeṭubhe  padakā veyyākaraṇā saddhamme pāramiṅgatā   ApTha                        TherāpadānaUppādesu nimittesu lakkhaṇesu ca kovidā  paṭṭhābhummantalikkhe te mama sissā susikkhitā   ApTha Appicchā nipakā ete appāhārā aloḷupā  lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā parivārenti maṃ sadā   ApTha Jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā santacittā samāhitā  ākiñcañaṃ patthayantā parivārenti maṃ sadā   ApTha Abhiññāpāramīpattā pettike gocare ratā  antalikkhacarā dhīrā parivārenti maṃ sadā   ApTha Saṃvutā chasu dvāresu anejā rakkhitindriyā  asaṃsaṭṭhā ca te dhīrā mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha Pallaṅkena nisajjāya thānā caṅkamanena ca  vītināmenti te rattiṃ mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha Rajanīye na rajjanti dosanīye na dussare  mohanīye na muyhanti mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha Iddhivīmaṃsamānā te vattanti niccakālikaṃ  paṭhaviṃ te pakampenti sārambhena durāsadā   ApTha Kīḷamānā ca te sissā kīḷanti jhānakīḷitaṃ  jambuto phalam ānenti mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha Aññe gacchanti Goyānaṃ aññe Pubbavidehanaṃ aññe Uttarakuruṃ ca mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha Purato khāriṃ pesenti pacchato ca vajanti te  catuvīsaṃsahassehi chāditaṃ hoti ambaraṃ   ApTha Aggipākī anaggī ca dantodukkhalikā pi ca  asmena koṭṭhikā keci pavattaphalabhojanā   ApTha Udakorohakā keci sāyaṃ pāto suciratā  toyābhisekacaraṇā mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha Parūḷhakacchanakhalomā paṅkadantā rajassirā  gandhitā sīlagandhena mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha  Sāriputta                    Pāto va sannipātetvā jaṭilā uggatāpanā  labhālabhaṃ pakittetvā gacchanti ambare tadā   ApTha Etesaṃ pakkamantānaṃ mahāsaddo pavattati  ajinacammasaddena moditā honti devatā   ApTha Disodisaṃ pakkamanti antalikkhacarā isī  sakabalen upatthaddhā te gacchanti yadicchakaṃ   ApTha Pathavīkampakā ete sabbe va nabhacārino  uggatejā duppasahā sāgaro va akkhobhiyā   ApTha Ṭhānacaṅkamiyā keci keci nesajjikā isī  pavattabhojanā keci mama sissā durāsadā   ApTha Mettāvihārino ete hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ  anattukkaṃsakā sabbe na te vambhenti kassaci   ApTha Sīharājā va sambhīto gajarājā va thāmavā  durāsadā vyagghariva agacchanti mam antike   ApTha Vijjādharā ca devatā nāgagandhabbarakkhasā  kumbhaṇḍā dānavā garuḷā upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Te jaṭā khāribhārikā ajinuttaravasino  antalikkhacarā sabbe upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ   ApTha Tadānucchavikā ete aññamaññaṃ sagāravā  catubbīsaṃsahassānaṃ khittasaddo na vijjati   ApTha Pāde pādaṃ nikkhipantā appasaddā susaṃvutā  upasaṅkamma sabbe va sirasā vandare mamaṃ   ApTha Tehi sissehi parivuto santehi ca tapassihi  vasāmi assame tattha jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ   ApTha Isīnaṃ sīlagandhena pupphagandhena cūbhayaṃ  phalinaṃ phalagandhena gandhito hoti assamo   ApTha Rattindivaṃ na jānāmi arati me na vijjati  sake sisse ovadanto bhiyyo hāsaṃ labhām ahaṃ   ApTha Pupphānaṃ pupphamānānaṃ phalānaṃ cāpi paccataṃ  dibbā gandhā pavāyanti sobhayantā mam assamaṃ   ApTha                     TherāpadānaSamādhimhā vuṭṭhahitvā ātāpī nipako ahaṃ  khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna vanam ajjhogahiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Uppāde supine cāpi lakkhaṇe susikkhito  pavattamānaṃ mantapadaṃ dharayāmi ahaṃ tadā   ApTha Anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  vivekakāmo sambuddho Himavantam upāgamī   ApTha Ajjhogahetvā Himavantam aggo kāruṇiko muni  pallaṅkam ābhujitvāna nisīdi purisuttamo   ApTha Tatth addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ sappabhāsaṃ manoramaṃ  indīvaraṃ va jalitaṃ ādittaṃ va hutāsanaṃ   ApTha Jalantaṃ dīparukkhaṃ va vijjuṃ abbhaghane yathā  suphullaṃ sālarājaṃ va addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha Ayaṃ nāgo mahāvīro dukkhass antakaro muni  idaṃ dassanam āgamma sabbe dukkhā pamuccare   ApTha Disvān ahaṃ devadevaṃ lakkhaṇam upadhārayiṃ  ‘Buddho nu kho na vā Buddho Handa passāmi cakkhumaṃ   ApTha Sahassārāni cakkāni dissanti caraṇuttame  lakkhaṇāni ssa disvāna niṭṭhaṃ gacchiṃ Tathāgate   ApTha Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna sammajjitvān ahaṃ tadā  aṭṭha pupphe samānetva buddhaseṭṭham apūjayiṃ   ApTha Pūjayitvāna taṃ buddhaṃ oghatiṇṇaṃ anāsavaṃ  ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā namassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha Yena ñāṇena sambuddho viharati anāsavo  taṃ ñāṇaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato   ApTha Samuddharas imaṃ lokaṃ sayambhu amitodaya  tava dassanam āgamma kaṅkhāsotaṃ taranti te   ApTha Tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ  parāyano patiṭṭhā ca dīpo ca dipaduttamo   ApTha Sakkā samudde udakaṃ pametum āḷhakena vā  na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   ApTha Dhāretuṃ pathaviṃ sakkā ṭhapetvā tulamaṇḍale  na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   ApTha  Sāriputta                  Ākāsaṃ minituṃ sakkā rajjuyā aṅgulena vā  na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   ApTha Mahāsamudde udakaṃ paṭhaviṃ cākhilañ jahe  buddhañāṇaṃ upādāya upamā te na yujjare   ApTha Sadevakassa lokassa cittaṃ yesaṃ pavattati  antojālagatā ete tava ñāṇamhi cakkhumā   ApTha Yena ñāṇena patto si kevalaṃ bodhim uttamaṃ  tena ñāṇena sabbaññū maddasi paratitthiye   ApTha Imā gāthā paṭhitvāna Suruci nāma tāpaso  ajinaṃ pattharitvāna paṭhaviyaṃ nisīdi so   ApTha Cullāsītisahassāni ajjhogāḷho mahaṇṇave  accuggato tāvad eva girirājā pavuccati   ApTha Tāva accuggato Neru āyato vitthato ca so  cuṇṇito aṇubhedena koṭisatasahassiyo   ApTha lakkhe ṭhapīyamānamhi parikkhayam agacchatha  na tveva tava sabbaññū ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave   ApTha Sukhumacchikena jālena udakaṃ yo parikkhipe  ye keci udake pāṇā antojālagatā siyuṃ   ApTha Tath eva hi mahāvīra ye keci puthutitthiyā  ditthīgahanapakkhannā parāmasena mohitā   ApTha Tava suddhena ñāṇena anāvaraṇadassinā  antojālagatā ete ñāṇaṃ te nātivattare   ApTha Bhagavā ca tamhi samaye Anomadassī mahāyaso  vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā disaṃ olokayī jino   ApTha Anomadassīmunino Nisabho nāma sāvako  parivuto satasahassehi santacittehi tādihi   ApTha Khīṇāsavehi suddhehi chaḷabhiññehi tādihi  cittam aññāya buddhassa upesi lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha Antalikkhe ṭhitā tattha padakkhiṇam akaṃsu te  namassantā pañjalikā orohuṃ buddhasantike   ApTha Anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā sitaṃ pātukarī jino   ApTha Varuṇo nām upaṭṭhāko sabbaññussa mahesino  ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā apucchi lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha                    TherāpadānaKo nu kho bhagavā hetu sitakammassa satthuno  na hi buddhā ahetuhi sitaṃ pātukaronti te   ApTha Anomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  saṅghamajjhe nisīditvā imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha   ApTha Yo maṃ pupphena pūjesi ñāṇañ cāpi anutthunī  tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato   ApTha Buddhassa giram aññāya sabbe devā samāgatā  saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te sambuddham upasaṅkamuṃ   ApTha Dasasu lokadhātūsu devakāyā mahiddhikā  saddhammaṃ sotukāmā te sambuddham upasaṅkamuṃ   ApTha Hatthī assā rathā pattī senā ca caturaṅginī  parivārenti taṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhiṃturiyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatā  upaṭṭhissanti taṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Soḷasitthisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā  vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā   ApTha Aḷārapamhāhasulā susoññā tanumajjhimā  parivārenti taṃ niccaṃ buddhapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Kappasatasahassāni devaloke ramissati  sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavattī rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati   ApTha Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  ApTha Pacchime bhave sampatte manussattaṃ gamissati  brāhmaṇī Sāriyā nāma dhārayissati kucchinā   ApTha Mātuyā nāmagottena paññāyissati yaṃ naro  Sāriputto ti nāmena tikkhapañño bhavissati   ApTha Asītikoṭī chaḍḍetvā pabbajissati kiñcano  gavesanto santipadaṃ carissati mahim imaṃ   ApTha Aparimeyye ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāmagottena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  Sāriputto ti nāmena hessati aggasāvako   ApTha  Sāriputta                   Ayaṃ Bhāgīrasī Gaṅgā Himavantā pabhāvita  mahāsamuddaṃ appeti tappayantī mahodadhiṃ   ApTha Tath evāyaṃ Sāriputto Sāketīsu visārado  paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā tappayissati pāṇino   ApTha Himavantam upādāya sāgarañ ca mahodadhiṃ  etthantare yaṃ puliṇaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  ApTha Tam pi sakkā asesena saṅkhātuṃ gaṇanā yathā  na tveva Sāriputtassa paññāy anto bhavissati   ApTha Lakkhe ṭhapīyamānamhi khīye Gaṅgāya vālukā  na tveva Sāriputtassa paññāy anto bhavissati   ApTha Mahāsamudde ūmiyo gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyā  tath eva Sāriputtassa paññāy anto na hessati   ApTha Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ Gotamaṃ Sakyapuṅgavaṃ  paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā hessati aggasāvako   ApTha Pavattitaṃ dhammacakkaṃ Sakyaputtena tādinā  anuvattessati sammā vassanto dhammavuṭṭhiyo   ApTha Sabbam etam abhiññāya Gotamo Sakyapuṅgavo  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati  ApTha Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ Anomadassissa satthuno  yassāhaṃ kāraṃ katvāna sabbattha pāramiṅgato   ApTha Aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha  sumutto saravego va kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto nibbānaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ  vicinaṃ titthiye sabbe esāhaṃ saṃsariṃ bhave   ApTha Yathāpi vyādhito poso pariyeseyya osadhaṃ  vicineyyā vanaṃ sabbaṃ vyādhino parimuttiyā   ApTha asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto nibbānaṃ amataṃ padaṃ  avyākiṇṇaṃ pañcasataṃ pabbajiṃ isipabbajjaṃ   ApTha Jaṭābhārena bharito ajinuttaranivās ahaṃ  abhiññāpāramiṃ gantvā brahmalokaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApTha                       TherāpadānaN atthi bāhirake buddhī ṭhapetvā jinasāsanaṃ  ye keci buddhimā sattā bujjhanti jinasāsanaṃ  ApTha Atthakāmaṃ mamam etaṃ nayidaṃ iti haṃ tadā  asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto kutitthaṃ sañcarim ahaṃ   ApTha Yathā sāratthiko poso kadaliṃ chetvā phālaye  na tattha sāraṃ vindeyyā sārena rittako hi so   ApTha Tath eva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhī bahujjanā  asaṅkhatena rittā va sārena kadalī yathā   ApTha Pacchime bhave sampatte brahmabandhu ahos ahaṃ  koṭiyo sataṃ chaḍḍayitvā pabbajim anāgāriyaṃ   ApTha PaṭhamakabhāṇavāraṃAjjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū  brāhmaṇo Sañjayo nāma tassa mūle vasām ahaṃ   ApTha Sāvako te mahāvīra Assaji nāma brāhmaṇo  durāsado uggatejo piṇḍāya carati sadā   ApTha Tam addasāsiṃ sappaññaṃ muniṃ mone samāhitaṃ  santacittaṃ mahānāgaṃ suphullaṃ padumaṃ yathā   ApTha Disvā me cittaṃ uppajji sudantaṃ suddhamānasaṃ  usabhaṃ pavaraṃ vīraṃ arahāyaṃ bhavissati   ApTha Pāsādiko iriyati abhirūpo susaṃvuto  uttame damathe danto amatadassī bhavissati   ApTha Yannūnāhaṃ uttamatthaṃ puccheyyaṃ tuṭṭhamānasaṃ  so me puṭṭho kathessati paṭipucchām ahaṃ tadā   ApTha Piṇḍacāraṃ carantassa pacchato agamās ahaṃ  okāsaṃ paṭimānento pucchituṃ amataṃ padaṃ   ApTha Vīthantare anuppattaṃ upagantvā apucchi haṃ  Kathaṃ gotto si tvaṃ dhīra kassa sisso si marisa   ApTha So me puṭṭho vyākāsi asambhīto va kesarī  Buddho loke samuppanno tassa sisso mhi sāvako   ApTha  Sāriputta                   Kīdisaṃ te mahāvīra anujātamahāyaso  buddhassa sāsanaṃ dhammaṃ sādhu me kathayass ubho   ApTha So me puṭṭho kathī sabbaṃ gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ padaṃ  taṇhasallassa hantāraṃ sabbadukkhapanūdanaṃ   ApTha Ye dhammā hetuppabhavā tesaṃ hetuṃ Tathāgato āha  tesañ ca yo nirodho evaṃ vādi mahāsamaṇo   ApTha So haṃ vissajjite pañhe paṭhamaṃ phalaṃ ajjhagaṃ virajo vimalo āsiṃ sutvāna jinasāsanaṃ   ApTha Sutvāna munino vākyaṃ passitvā dhammaṃ uttamaṃ  pariyogāḷhasaddhammo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhās ahaṃ   ApTha ‘Es eva dhammo yadi tāvad eva paccavyathā padam asokaṃ  adiṭṭham abbhatītaṃ bahukehi kappanahutehi   ApTha Sāhaṃ dhammaṃ gavesanto kutitthe sañcarim ahaṃ  so me attho anuppatto kālo me na ppamajjituṃ   ApTha Tosito haṃ Assajinā patvāna acalaṃ padaṃ  sahāyakaṃ gavesanto assamam agamās ahaṃ   ApTha Dūrato va mamaṃ disvā sahāyo me susikkhito  iriyāpathasampanno idaṃ vacanam abravī   ApTha Pasannamukhanetto si muni munibhāvo va dissati  amatādhigato kacci nibbānaṃ accutaṃ padaṃ   ApTha Subhānurūpo āyāsi anejjaṅkārito viya  danto ca uttamadamathe upasanto si brāhmaṇa   ApTha Amataṃ mayā dhigataṃ sokasallavinodanaṃ  tuvam pi adhigacche hi gacchāma buddhasantikaṃ   ApTha Sādhū ti so paṭissutvā sahāyo me susikkhito  hatthena hatthaṃ gaṇhitvā upāgamī satthusantikaṃ  ApTha Ubho pi pabbajissāma Sakyaputta tav antike  tava sāsanam āgamma viharāma anāsavā   ApTha Kolito iddhiyā seṭṭho ahaṃ paññāya pārago  ubho ca ekato hutvā sāsanaṃ sobhayāmase   ApTha                     TherāpadānaApariyositasaṅkappo kutitthe sañcarim ahaṃ  tava dassanam āgamma saṅkappo pūrito mama   ApTha Paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya pupphanti samaye dumā  dibbā gandhā sampavanti tosenti sabbapāṇinaṃ   ApTha Tath evāhaṃ mahāvīra Sakyaputta mahāyasa  sāsane te patiṭṭhāya samay esāmi pupphituṃ   ApTha Vimuttipuppham esanto bhavasaṃsāramocanaṃ  vimuttipupphalābhena tosemi sabbapāṇinaṃ   ApTha Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi ṭhapetvāna mahāmuniṃ  paññāya sadiso n atthi tava puttassa cakkhumā   ApTha Suvinītā ca te sissā parisā ca susikkhitā  uttame damathe dantā parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Jhāyī jhānaratā dhīrā santacittā samāhitā  munī moneyyasampannā parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Appicchā nipakā dhīrā appāhārā alolupā  lābhālabhena santuṭṭhā parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Āraññakā dhutaratā jhāyino lūkhacīvarā  vivekābhiratā dhīrāparivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Paṭipannā phalaṭṭhā ca sekhā phalasamaṅgino  āsiṃsakā uttamatthaṃ parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Sotāpannā ca vimalā sakadāgāmino ca ye  anāgāmī ca arahā parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Satipaṭṭhānakusalā bojjhaṅgābhāvanāratā  sāvakā te bahū sabbe parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Iddhipādesu kusalā samādhibhāvanāratā  sammappadhānam anuyuktā parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca iddhiyā pāramiṅgatā  paññāya pāramīpattā parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Edisā te mahāvīra tava sissā susikkhitā  durāsadā uggatejā parivārenti taṃ sadā   ApTha Tehi sissehi parivuto saññatehi tapassihi  migarājā v asambhīto uḷurājā va sobhasi   ApTha Paṭhaviyaṃ patiṭṭhāya ruhanti dharaṇīruhā  vepullataṃ papuṇanti phalan ca dassayanti te   ApTha  Sāriputta                    Paṭhavī sadiso tvaṃ si Sakyaputta mahāyasa  sāsane te patiṭṭhāya labhanti amataṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Sindhū Sarasvatī c eva nadiyā Candabhāgiyo  Gaṅgā ca Yamunā c eva Sarabhū ca atho Mahī  ApTha Etāsaṃ sandamānānaṃ sāgaro sampaṭicchati  jahanti purimaṃ nāmaṃ sāgaro te va ñāyati  ApTha Tath ev ime catuvaṇṇā pabbajitvā tav antike  jahanti purimaṃ nāmam buddhaputtā ti ñāyare   ApTha Yathāpi cando vimalo gacchaṃ ākāsadhātuyā  sabbe tārāgaṇe loke ābhāya atirocati   ApTha Tath eva tvaṃ mahāvīra parivuto devamānuse  buddhakhettaṃ atikkamma jalasi sabbadā tuvaṃ   ApTha Gambhīre uṭṭhitā ūmi na velam ativattati  sabbavelam paphusanti sañcuṇṇā vikiranti tā   ApTha Tath eva titthiyā loke nānādiṭṭhī bahujjanā  dhammaṃ dhāritukāmā te n ātivattanti taṃ muniṃ   ApTha Sac eva taṃ pāpuṇanti paṭivādehi cakkhuma  tav antikaṃ upāgantvā sañcuṇṇā va bhavanti te   ApTha Yathāpi udake jātā kumudā mandālakā bahū  upalimpanti toyena kaddamakalalena ca   ApTha Tath eva bahukā sattā loke jātā virūhare  aṭṭitā rāgadosena kaddame kumudaṃ yathā   ApTha Yathā padumaṃ jalajaṃ jalamajjhe virūhati  na so limpati toyena parisuddho hi kesarī   ApTha Tath eva tvaṃ mahāvīra loke jāto mahāmuni  no palimpasi lokena toyena padumaṃ yathā   ApTha Yathāpi rammake māse bahū pupphanti vārijā  nātikkamanti taṃ māsaṃ samayo pupphanāya so   ApTha                      TherāpadānaTath eva tvaṃ Sakyaputta pupphitā te vimuttiyā  sāsanaṃ nātivattanti padumaṃ vārijaṃ yathā   ApTha Supupphito sālarājā dibbagandhaṃ pavāyati  aññasālehi parivuto sālarājā va sobhati   ApTha Tath eva tvaṃ mahāvīra buddhañāṇena pupphito  bhikkhusaṅghena parivuto sālarājā va sobhasi  ApTha Yathāpi selo Himavā osadho sabbapāṇinaṃ  nāgānam asurānañ ca devatānañ ca ālayo   ApTha Tath eva tvaṃ mahāvīra osadho viya pāṇinaṃ  tevijjā chaḷabhiññā ca iddhiyā pāramiṅgatā   ApTha Anusiṭṭhā mahāvīra tayā kāruṇikena te  ramanti dhammaratiyā vasanti tava sāsane   ApTha Migarājā yathā sīho abhinikkhamma āsayā  catuddisā viloketvā tikkhattuṃ abhinādayi   ApTha Sabbe migā uttasanti migarājassa gajjato  tathā hi jātimā eso pasu tāseti sabbadā   ApTha Gajjato te mahāvīra vasudhā sampakampati  bodhaneyyā va bojjhanti tasanti mārakāyikā   ApTha Tasanti titthiyā sabbe nadato te mahāmuni  kākasenā va vibbhantā migaraññā yathā migā   ApTha Ye keci gaṇino loke satthāro ti pavuccare  paramparāgataṃ dhammaṃ desenti parisāya te   ApTha Na h eva tvaṃ mahāvīra dhammaṃ desesi pāṇinaṃ  samaṃ saccāni bujjhitvā kevalaṃ bodhipakkhikaṃ   ApTha Āsayānusayaṃ ñatvā indriyānaṃ phalāphalaṃ bhabbābhabbe viditvāna mahāmegho va gajjasi   ApTha Cakkavālapariyantā nisinnā parisā bhave  nānādiṭṭhī vicintenti vimaticchedanāya taṃ   ApTha  Sāriputta                Sabbesaṃ cittam aññāya opammakusalo muni  ekaṃ pañhaṃ kathento va vimatin chindi pāṇinaṃ   ApTha Upadisasadiseh eva vāsudhā pūritā bhave  sabbe va te pañjalikā kittayuṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha Kappaṃ vā te kittayantā nānāvaṇṇehi kittayuṃ  parimetuṃ na pappeyyum appameyyo Tathāgato   ApTha Yathā sakena thāmena kittito hi mahājino  kappakoṭī pakittentā evamevam akittayuṃ   ApTha Sace hi koci devo vā manusso vā susikkhito  pūritaṃ parikaḍḍheyya vighātaṃ va labheyya so   ApTha Sāsane te patiṭṭhāya Sakyaputta mahāyasa  paññāya pāramiṃ gantvā viharāmi anāsavo   ApTha Titthiye sampamaddāmi vattemi jinasāsanaṃ  dhammasenāpati ajja Sakyaputtassa sāsane   ApTha Aparimeyye kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha  sukhito saravego va kilese jhāpayī mamaṃ  ApTha Yo koci manujo bhāraṃ dhāreyya matthake sadā  bhārena dukkhito assa bhāro hi bharito tathā   ApTha Dayhamāno tīhaggīhi bhavesu saṃsariṃ ahaṃ  bharito bhavabhārena girim uccārito yathā   ApTha Oropito ca me bhāro bhavā ugghāṭitā mayā  karaṇīyaṃ kataṃ sabbaṃ Sakyaputtassa sāsane   ApTha Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi ṭhapetvā Sakyapuṅgavaṃ  aham aggo mhi paññāya sadiso me na vijjati   ApTha Samādhimhi sukusalo iddhiyā pāramiṅgato  icchamāno va haṃ ajja sahāyam abhinimmine   ApTha                    TherāpadānaAnupubbavihārissa vasībhūto mahāmuni kathesi sāsanaṃ mayhaṃ nirodho sayanaṃ mamaṃ  ApTha Dibbacakkhuṃ visuddham me samādhikusalo ahaṃ  sammappadhānam anuyutto bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato   ApTha Sāvakena hi pattabbaṃ sabbam eva kataṃ mamaṃ lokanāthaṃ ṭhapetvāna sadiso me na vijjati   ApTha Samāpattivinayakusalo jhānavimokkhānaṃ khippalābhī  bojjhaṅgabhāvanārato sāvakaguṇapāramiṅgato smiṃ   ApTha Sāvakaguṇenāpi phusena buddhiyā purisuttamagāravā  saddhāya saṅgahītaṃ cittaṃ sadā sabrahmacārisu  ApTha Uddhataviso va sappo chinnavisāno va usabho  nikkhittamānadappo upemi garugāravena gaṇaṃ   ApTha Yadi rūpinī bhaveyya paññā me vasupatīnaṃ sameyya  Anomadassissa bhagavato phalam etaṃ ñāṇaṃ thavanāya  ApTha Pavattitaṃ dhammacakkaṃ Sakyaputtena tādinā  anuvattem ahaṃ sammā ñāṇathavanāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Mā me kadāci pāpiccho kusīto hīnavīriyo  appassuto anācāro sameto katthaci ahu   ApTha Bahussuto ca medhāvī sīlesu susamāhito  cetosamathānuyukto api muddhani tiṭṭhatu   ApTha Taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddante yāvant ettha samāgatā  appicchā hotha santuṭṭhā jhāyī jhānaratā sadā   ApTha  MahāMoggallāna                 Yam ahaṃ paṭhamaṃ disvā virajo vimalo ahuṃ  so me ācariyo vīro Assaji nāma sāvako   ApTha Tassāhaṃ vāhasā ajja dhammasenāpatī ahuṃ  sabbattha pāramiṃ patvā viharāmi anāsavo   ApTha Yo me ācariyo āsi Assaji nāma sāvako  yassaṃ disāyaṃ vasati ussīsamhikaro ahaṃ   ApTha Mama kammaṃ saritvāna Gotamo Sakyapuṅgavo  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ   ApTha Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḍābhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsasanaṃ ti   ApTha Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Sāriputto thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiSāriputtattherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃAnomadassī bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  vihāsi Himavantamhi devasaṅghapurakkhato   ApTha Varūṇo nāma nāmena nāgarājā ahaṃ tadā  kāmarūpī vikubbāmi mahodadhi nivās ahaṃ   ApTha Saṅganiyaṃ gaṇaṃ hitvā turiyaṃ paṭṭhapes ahaṃ  sambuddhaṃ parivāretvā vādesuṃ accharā tadā   ApTha Vajjamānesu turiyesu devā turiyāni vajjiṃsu  ubhiṇṇaṃ saddaṃ sutvāna buddho pi sampabujjhatha   ApTha Nimantayitvā sambuddhaṃ sakaṃ bhavanam upāgamiṃ āsanaṃ paññapetvāna kālam ārocayim ahaṃ   ApTha Khīṇāsavasahassehi purato lokanāyako  obhāsento disā sabbā bhavanam me upāgami   ApTha                    TherāpadānaUpaviṭṭhaṃ mahāvīraṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ  bhikkhusaṅghaṃ santappesiṃ annapānen ahaṃ tadā   ApTha Anumodi mahāvīro sayambhu aggapuggalo  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha Yo so saṅghaṃ apūjesi buddhañ ca lokanāyakaṃ  tena cittappasādena devalokaṃ gamissati   ApTha Sattasattatikkhattuñ ca devarajjaṃ karissati  paṭhavyarajjaṃ aṭṭhasataṃ vasudham āvasissati   ApTha Pañcapaññāsakkhattuṃ ca cakkavatti bhavissati  bhogā asaṅkhiyā tassa uppajjissanti tāvade   ApTha Aparimeyye ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Nirayā so cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati  Kolito nāma nāmena brahmabandhu bhavissati   ApTha So pacchā pabbajitvāna kusalamūlena codito  Gotamassa bhagavato dutiyo hessati sāvako   ApTha Āraddhavīriyo pahitatto iddhiyā pāramiṅgato  sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat anāsavo   ApTha Pāpamittopanissāya kāmarāgavasaṅgato  mātaraṃ pitaraṃ cāpi ghātayiṃ duṭṭhamānaso   ApTha Yaṃ yaṃ yon upapajjāmi nirayaṃ atha mānusaṃ  pāpakammasamaṅgīnaṃ bhinnasīso bhavām ahaṃ   ApTha Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ carimo vattate bhavo  idhāpi ca disaṃ mayhaṃ maraṇakāle bhavissati   ApTha Pavivekaṃ anuyutto samādhibhāvanārato  sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   ApTha Dharaṇiṃ pi sugambhīraṃ bahalaṃ duppadhaṃsiyaṃ  vāmaṅguṭṭhena khobheyyam iddhiyā pāramiṃgato  ApTha Asmimānaṃ na passāmi māno mayhaṃ na vijjati  sāmaṇere upādāya garucittaṃ karom ahaṃ   ApTha Aparimeyye ito kappe yaṃ kammaṃ abhinīhariṃ  tāhaṃ bhumiṃ anuppatto patto mhi āsavakkhayaṃ   ApTha  MahāKassapa                    Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   ApTha Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Mahāmoggallāno thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiMahāmoggallānattherassa  apadānaṃsamattaṃPadumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  nibbute lokanāthamhi pūjaṃ kubbanti satthuno  udaggacittā janatā āmoditapamoditā   ApTha Tesu saṃvegajātesu pīti me udapajjatha Agghiyaṃ sukataṃ katvā satahatthaṃ samuggataṃ  diyaḍḍhaṃ hatthasataṃ pi vimānaṃ nabham uggataṃ   ApTha Katvāna agghiyaṃ tattha tālapantīhi cittitaṃ  sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā cetiyaṃ pūjay uttamaṃ   ApTha Aggikkhandho va jalito sālarājā va phullito  indalaṭṭhīva ākāse obhāseti catuddisā   ApTha Tesu cittaṃ pasādetvā katvāna kusalaṃ bahuṃ  pubbakammaṃ saritvāna tidasaṃ upapajj ahaṃ   ApTha                       ApadānaSahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ dibbaṃ yānam adhiṭṭhito  ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ sattabhūmi samuggataṃ   ApTha Kūṭāgārasahassāni sabbe sovaṇṇayā ahuṃ jalanti sakatejena disā sabbā pabhāsayaṃ   ApTha Santi aññe pi niyyuhā lohitaṅkamayā tadā  te pi jotanti ābhāya samantā caturo disā   ApTha Puññakammābhinibbattā kūṭāgārā sunimmitā  maṇimayāpi jotanti disādasa samantato   ApTha Tesaṃ ujjotamānānaṃ obhāso vipulo ahu  sabbe deve atibhomi puññakammass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhikappasahassamhi Ubbiddho nāma khattiyo  caturanto vijitāvī puṭhaviṃ āvasiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Tamh eva bhaddake kappe tiṃsakkhattuṃ ahos ahaṃ  sakakammābhiraddho mhi cakkavatti mahabbalo  ApTha Sattaratanasampanno cātudīpamhi issaro  tatthāpi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ indalaṭṭhi va uggataṃ   ApTha Āyāmato catubbīsaṃ vitthārena ca dvādasā  Rammakaṃ nāma naṅgaraṃ daḷhapākāratoraṇaṃ   ApTha Āyāmato pañcasataṃ vitthārena tadaḍḍhakaṃ  ākiṇṇaṃ janakāyehi tidasānaṃ puraṃ viya   ApTha Yathā sucighare Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   ApTha Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Mahākassapo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiMahākassapatherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃSumedhaṃ bhagavantāhaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  vupakaṭṭhaṃ viharantaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  añjalim paggahetvāna buddhaseṭṭham ayāc ahaṃ   ApTha ‘Anukampī mahāvīra lokajeṭṭha narāsabha  padīpan te padassāmi rukkhamūlamhi jhāyato  ApTha Adhivāsesi so dhīro sayambhū vadataṃ varo  dumesu vinivijjhitvā yantaṃ yojetv ahaṃ tadā   ApTha Sahassavaṭṭiṃ pādāsiṃ buddhassa lokabandhuno  sattāhaṃ pajjalitvāna padīpā vupasammisuṃ  ApTha Tena cittappasādena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ vimānaṃ upapajj ahaṃ  ApTha Upapannassa devattaṃ thambho āsi sunimmito  samantato pajjalati dīpadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha                     ApadānaSamantā yojanaṃ sabbaṃ virocemi ahaṃ tadā  sabbe deve atihomi dīpadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Tiṃsakappāni devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ  na maṃ kec atimaññanti dīpadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Aṭṭhavīsatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī ahos ahaṃ  divārattiñ ca passāmi samantā yojanaṃ tadā   ApTha Sahassalokaṃ ñāṇena passāmi satthu sāsane  dibbacakkhuṃ anuppatto dīpadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Sumedho nāma sambuddho tiṃsakappasahass ito  tassa dīpo mayā dinno vippasannena cetasā   ApTha ApTha Tāhaṃ dhammaṃ suṇitvāna abhivādetvāna satthuno  añjalim paggahetvāna pakkāmiṃ dakkhiṇāmukho   ApTha Saṅkhittena suṇitvāna vitthārena adesayiṃ sabbe sissā attamanā sutvāna mama bhāsato   ApTha Sakadiṭṭhiṃ vinodetvā buddhe cittaṃ pasādayuṃ  saṅkhittena pi desemi vitthārena tath ev ahaṃ   ApTha  Upāli                     Abhidhammanayañño haṃ Kathāvatthuvisuddhiyā  sabbesaṃ viññāpetvāna viharāmi anāsavo   ApTha Ito pañcasate kappe caturo suppakāsakā  sattaratanasampannā cātuddīpamhi issarā   ApTha Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanan ti   ApTha Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Puṇṇomantāniputtothero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthātiPuṇṇo Mantāṇiputtattherassa apadānaṃsamattaṃNaṅgare Haṃsavatiyā Sujāto nāma brāhmaṇo  asītikoṭinicayo pahūtadhanadhaññavā   ApTha Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragū  lakkhaṇe itibhāse ca saddhamme pāramiṅgato   ApTha Paribbājā ekasikhā Gotamabuddhasāvakā  carakā tāpasā c eva caranti mahiyā tadā   ApTha ‘Te pi maṃ parivārenti brāhmaṇo vissuto iti  bahujjano maṃ pūjeti nāhaṃ pūjemi kañcinaṃ  ApTha Pūjārahaṃ na passāmi mānatthaddho ahaṃ tadā  buddho ti vacanaṃ natthi tāva nuppajjate jino   ApTha Accayena ahorattaṃ Padumuttaranāyako  sabbaṃ tamaṃ vinodetvā loke uppajji cakkhumā   ApTha Vitthārike bahujaññe puthubhūte ca sāsane  upāgami tadā buddho naṅgaraṃ Haṃsasavhayaṃ  ApTha                    ApadānaParūpatthāya so buddhodhammaṃ desesi cakkhumā  tena kālena parisā samantā yojanaṃ tadā   ApTha Sammato manujānaṃ so Sunando nāma tāpaso  yāvatā buddhaparisā puppheh acchādayī tadā   ApTha Catusaccaṃ pakāsento seṭṭhe va pupphamaṇḍape  koṭisatasahassānaṃ dhammābhisamayo ahu   ApTha Sattarattindivaṃ buddho vassitvā dhammavuṭṭhiyā  aṭṭhame divase patte Sunandaṃ kittayi jino   ApTha Devaloke manusse vā saṃsaranto ayaṃ bhave  sabbesaṃ pavaro hutvā bhaveussaṃsarissati   ApTha Kappasatasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  Mantāṇiputto Puṇṇo ti hessati satthu sāvako   ApTha Evaṃ kittayi sambuddho Sunandaṃ tāpasaṃ tadā  hāsayanto janaṃ sabbaṃ dassayanto sakaṃ balaṃ   ApTha Katañjalī namassanti Sunandaṃ tāpasaṃ tadā  buddhe kāraṃ karitvāna sodhesi gatim attano   ApTha Tattha me ahu saṅkappo sutvāna munino vacaṃ aham pi kāraṃ karissāmi yathā passāmi Gotamaṃ   ApTha Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna kiriyaṃ cintayiṃ mamaṃ kyāhaṃ kammaṃ ācarāmi puññakkhette anuttare   ApTha Ayaṃ ca pāṭhiko bhikkhu sabbapāṭhikasāsane  vinaye agganikkhitto taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthaye ahaṃ   ApTha Idaṃ me amitaṃ bhogaṃ akkhobhaṃ sāgarūpamaṃ  tena bhogena buddhassa ārāmaṃ māpaye ahaṃ   ApTha Sobhanaṃ nāma ārāmaṃ naṅgarassa puratthato  katvā satasahassena saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ  ApTha  Upāli                   Kūṭāgāre ca pāsāde maṇḍape kammiye guhā  caṅkame sukate katvā saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ   ApTha Jantāgharaṃ aggisālaṃ adho udakamālakaṃ  nahānagharaṃ māpayitvā bhikkhusaṅghass adās ahaṃ   ApTha Āsandiyo pīṭhake ca paribhoge ca bhājane  ārāmikañ ca bhesajjaṃ sabbam etaṃ adās ahaṃ   ApTha Ārakkhaṃ paṭṭhapetvāna pākāraṃ kārayiṃ daḷhaṃ  mā naṃ koci viheṭhesi santacittāna tādinaṃ   ApTha Āvāsasatasahassena saṅghārāmaṃ amāpayiṃ  vepullataṃ pāpayitvā sambuddhaṃ upanāmayiṃ  ApTha Niṭṭhāpito mayārāmo sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ muni  niyyātessāmi te vīra adhivāsehi cakkhumā   ApTha Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  mama saṅkappam aññāya adhivāsesi nāyako   ApTha Adhivāsanam aññāya sabbaññussa mahesino  bhojanaṃ paṭiyādetvā kālam ārocayiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Ārocitamhi kālamhi Padumuttaranāyako  khīṇāsavasahassehi ārāmaṃ me upāgami   ApTha Nisinnaṃ kālam aññāya annapānena tappayiṃ bhuttāviṃkālam aññāya idaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   ApTha ‘Kīto satasahassena tattaken eva kārito  Sobhano nāma ārāmo sampaṭiccha tuvaṃ mune  ApTha Iminārāmadānena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  bhave nibbattamāno haṃ labhāmi mama patthitaṃ   ApTha Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā idaṃ vacanam abravi  ApTha Yo so buddhassa pādāsi saṅghārāmaṃ sumāpitaṃ  tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   ApTha                         ApadānaHatthīassārathāpattī senā ca caturaṅginī  parivāressant imaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhiṃ turiyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatā  parivāressant imaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmass idan phalaṃ   ApTha Chalāsītisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā  vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā   ApTha Āḷārāpamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimā  parivāressant imaṃ niccaṃ saṅghārāmass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati  sahassakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati   ApTha Devarājena pattabbaṃ sabbaṃ paṭilabhissati  anūnabhogo hutvāna devarajjaṃ karissati   ApTha Sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavatti rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati  pathavyā rajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  ApTha Kappasatasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  Upāli nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   ApTha Vinaye pāramippatto ṭhānāṭhāne ca kovido  jinasāsanaṃ dhārento viharissat anāsavo  ApTha Sabbam etaṃ abhiññāya Gotamo Sakyapuṅgavo  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapessati   ApTha Aparimeyy upādāya patthemi tava sāsanaṃ  so me attho anuppatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo   ApTha Yathā sūlāvuto poso rājadaṇḍena tajjito  sūle sātaṃ na vindanto parimuttiṃ va icchati   ApTha Tath evāhaṃ mahāvīra bhavadaṇḍena tajjito  kammasūlāvuto santo pipāsāvedanāṭṭito   ApTha Bhave sātaṃ na vindāmi ḍayhanto tīhi aggihi  parimuttiṃ gavesāmi yathāpi rājadaṇḍito  ApTha  Upāli                     Yathā visādo puriso visena paripīḷito  agadaṃ so gaveseyya visaghātāy upāyaso  ApTha Gavesamāno passeyya agadaṃ visaghātakaṃ  tam pivitvā sukhī assa visamhā parimuttiyā   ApTha Tath evāhaṃ mahāvīra yathā visahato naro  sampīḷito avijjāya saddhammāgadaṃ esahaṃ   ApTha Dhammāgadhaṃ gavesanto addakkhiṃ Sākyasāsanaṃ  aggasabbosadhānaṃ taṃ sabbasallavinodanaṃ   ApTha Dhammosadhaṃ pivitvāna visaṃ sabbaṃ samūhaniṃ  ajarāmaraṃ sītibhāvaṃ nibbānaṃ passayiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Yathā bhūtaṭṭito poso bhūtaggāhena pīḷito  bhūtavejjaṃ gaveseyya bhūtasmā parimuttiyā   ApTha Gavesamāno passeyya bhūtavijjāsu kovidaṃ  tassa so vihaññe bhūtaṃ samūlañ ca vināsaye   ApTha Tath evāhaṃ mahāvīra tamaggāhena pīḷito  ñāṇalokaṃ gavesāmi tamato parimuttiyā   ApTha Ath addasaṃ Sakyamuniṃ kilesatamasodhanaṃ  so me tamaṃ vinodesi bhūtavejjo va bhūtikaṃ   ApTha Saṃsārasotaṃ sañchindiṃ taṇhāsotaṃ nivārayiṃ  bhavaṃ ugghāṭayiṃ sabbaṃ bhūtavejjo va mūlato   ApTha Garuḷo yathā opatti pannagaṃ bhakkham attano  samantāyojanasataṃ vikkhobheti mahāsaraṃ   ApTha Pannagaṃ so gahetvāna adhosīsaṃ viheṭhayaṃ ādāya so pakkamati yena kāmaṃ vihaṅgamo   ApTha Tath evāhaṃ mahāvīra yathāpi Garuḷo balī  asaṅkhataṃ gavesanto dose vikkhālayiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Diṭṭho ahaṃ dhammavaraṃ santipadam anuttaraṃ  ādāya viharām etaṃ Garuḷo pannagaṃ yathā   ApTha Āsāvatī nāma latā jātā cittalatāvane  tassā vassasahassena ekaṃ nibbattate phalaṃ   ApTha                        ApadānaTaṃ devā payirupāsanti tāva dūraphalaṃ satiṃ devānaṃ sā piyā evaṃ āsāvati latuttamā   ApTha Satasahassaṃ upādāya tāhaṃ paricare muniṃ  sāyaṃpātaṃ namassāmi devā āsāvatiṃ yathā   ApTha Avañjhā pāricariyā amoghā ca namassanā  dūrāgatam pi maṃ santaṃ khaṇo maṃ na virādhayi  ApTha Paṭisandhiṃ na passāmi vicinanto bhave ahaṃ  nirupadhi vippamutto upasanto carām ahaṃ   ApTha Yathāpi padumaṃ nāma sūraraṃsena pupphati  tath evāhaṃ mahāvīra buddharaṃsena pupphito   ApTha Yathā balākayonimhi na vijjati pumā sadā  meghesu gajjamānesu gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti tā sadā   ApTha Ciram pi gabbhaṃ dhārenti yāva megho na gajjati  bhārato parimuccanti yadā megho pavassati   ApTha Padumuttarabuddhassa dhammameghena gajjato  saddena dhammameghassa dhammagabbhaṃ agaṇhihaṃ  ApTha Satasahassaṃ upādāya puññagabbhaṃ dharem ahaṃ  nappamuccāmi bhārato dhammamegho na gajjati   ApTha Yadā tuvaṃ Sakyamuni ramme Kapilavatthave  gajjasi dhammameghena bhārato parimucc ahaṃ   ApTha Suññataṃ animittañ ca tathāpaṇihitam pi ca  caturo ca phale sabbe dhamme va vijaṭāy ahaṃ   ApTha DutiyabhāṇavāraṃAparimeyy upādāya patthemi tava sāsanaṃ  so me attho anuppatto santiṃ padam anuttaraṃ   ApTha  Upāli                     Vinaye pāramiṃ patto yathā pi pāṭhiko isi  na me samasamo atthi dhāremi sāsanaṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Vinaye khandhake cāpi tikacchede va pañcake  ettha me vimati n atthi akkhare vyañjane pi vā  ApTha Niggahe paṭikamme ca ṭhānāṭhāne ca kovido  osāraṇe vuṭṭhāpane sabbaṭṭha pāramiṅgato   ApTha Vinaye khandhake cāpi nikkhipitvā padaṃ ahaṃ  ubhato viniveṭhetvā rasato osāreyy ahaṃ   ApTha Niruttiyā ca kusalo atthānatthe ca kovido  anaññātaṃ mayā n atthi ekaggo satthu sāsane   ApTha Rūpadakkho ahaṃ ajja Sakyaputtassa sāsane  kaṅkhaṃ sabbaṃ vinodemi chindāmi sabbasaṃsayaṃ   ApTha Padaṃ anupadañ cāpi akkharañ cāpi vyañjanaṃ  nidāne pariyosāne sabbattha kovido ahaṃ   ApTha Yathāpi rājā balavā niggaṇhitvā paran tape  vijinitvāna saṅgāmaṃ naṅgaraṃ tattha māpaye   ApTha Pākāraṃ parikhañ cāpi esikañ dvārakoṭṭhakaṃ  aṭṭālake ca vividhe kāraye naṅgare bahū   ApTha Siṅghāṭakaṃ caccarañ ca suvibhattantarāpaṇaṃ  kārayeyya sabhaṃ tattha atthānatthaṃ vinicchayaṃ   ApTha Nigghāṭatthaṃ amittānaṃ chiddāchiddañ ca jānituṃ rakkhāya balakāyassa senāpaccam ṭhapeti so   ApTha Ārakkhatthāya bhaṇḍassa nidhānakusalaṃ naraṃ  ‘mā me bhaṇḍaṃ vinassī ti bhaṇḍarakkhaṃ ṭhapeti so   ApTha Māmako hoti yo rañño vuddhiṃ yassa ca icchati  tassādhikaraṇaṃ deti mittassa paṭipajjituṃ  ApTha Uppādesu nimittesu lakkhaṇesu ca kovidaṃ  ajjhāyakaṃ mantadharaṃ porohicce ṭhapeti so   ApTha                       ApadanaEteh aṅgehi sampanno khattiyo ti pavuccati  sadā rakkhanti rājānaṃ cakkavāko va dukkhitaṃ  ApTha Tath eva tvaṃ mahāvīra hatāmitto va khattiyo  sadevakassa lokassa dhammarājā ti vuccati  ApTha Titthiye nihanitvāna Mārañ cāpi sasenakaṃ  tam andhakāraṃ vidhamitvā dhammanaṅgaraṃ amāpayi  ApTha Sīlaṃ pākārikaṃ tattha ñāṇan te dvārakoṭṭhakaṃ  saddhā te esikā dhīra dvārapālo va saṃvaro   ApTha Satipaṭṭhānam aṭṭālaṃ paññā te caccaraṃ mune  iddhipādañ ca siṅghāṭaṃ dhammavīthiṃ sumāpitaṃ   ApTha Suttantaṃ Abhidhammañ ca Vinayañ cāpi kevalaṃ  navaṅgabuddhavacanaṃ ettha dhammasabhā tava  ApTha Suññatam animittañ ca vihārañ cāppanīhitaṃ  anejañ ca nirodho ca esā dhammakuṭi tava   ApTha Paññāya aggo nikkhitto paṭibhāne ca kovido  Sāriputto ti nāmena dhammasenāpatī tava   ApTha Cutūpapātakusalo iddhiyā pāramiṅgato  Kolito nāma nāmena porohicco tava mune   ApTha Porāṇakavaṃsadharo uggatejo durāsado  dhūtavādiguṇen aggo akkhadasso tavaṃ mune   ApTha Bahussuto dhammadharo sabbapāṭhī ca sāsane  Ānando nāma nāmena dhammārakkho tavaṃ mune   ApTha Ete sabbe atikkamma pihesi bhagavā mamaṃ vinicchayam me pādāsi vinaye viññūdesitaṃ   ApTha Yo koci vinaye pañhaṃ pucchati buddhasāvako  tattha me cintanā n atthi tañ yev atthaṃ kathem ahaṃ   ApTha Yāvatā buddhakhettamhi ṭhapetvā taṃ mabāmuni  vinaye mādiso n atthi kuto bhiyyo bhavissati   ApTha  Upāli                     Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā evaṃ gajjati Gotamo  Upālissa samo n atthi Vinaye Khandhakesu ca   ApTha Yāvatā Buddhabhaṇitaṃ navaṅgaṃ Satthusāsanaṃ  vinayogadhitaṃ sabbaṃ vinayamūlapassino  ApTha Mama kammaṃ saritvāna Gotamo Sakyapuṅgavo  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ   ApTha Satasahass upādāya imaṃ ṭhānaṃ apatthayiṃ so me attho anuppatto vinaye pāramiṅgato   ApTha Sakyānaṃ nandijanano kappako ās ahaṃ pure  vijahitvāna taṃ jātiṃ putto jāto mahesino   ApTha Ito dutiyake kappe Ajaso nāma khattiyo  anantatejo amitayaso bhūmipālo mahaddhano  ApTha Tassa rañño ahaṃ putto Candano nāma khattiyo  jātimaden upatthaddho yasabhogamadena ca   ApTha Nāgasatasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  tidhapabhinnā mātaṅgā parivārenti maṃ sadā   ApTha Sabalehi pareto haṃ uyyānaṃ gantukāmako  āruyha Sirikaṃ nāgaṃ naṅgarā nikkhamiṃ tadā   ApTha Caraṇena ca sampanno guttadvāresusaṃvuto  Devalo nāma sambuddho āgacchi purato mamaṃ  ApTha Pesetvā Sirikaṃ nāgaṃ Buddhaṃ āsādayiṃ tadā  tato sañjātakopo so nāgo nuddharate padaṃ   ApTha Nāgaṃ duṭṭhamanaṃ disvā Buddhe kopaṃ akās ahaṃ  vihesayitvā sambuddhaṃ uyyānaṃ agamās ahaṃ   ApTha Sātaṃ tattha na vindāmi siro pajjalito yathā  parilāhena ḍayhāmi maccho va baḷisādako  ApTha                         ApadānaSasāgarantā pathavī ādittā viya hoti me  pitu santik upāgamma idaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   ApTha Āsīvisaṃ va kupitaṃ aggikkhandham va āgataṃ  mattaṃ va kuñjaraṃ dantiṃ yaṃ sayambhuṃ asādayiṃ  ApTha Āsādito mayā Buddho ghoro uggatapo jino  purā sabbe vinassāma khamāpessāma taṃ muniṃ   ApTha No ce taṃ nijjhapessāma attadantaṃ samāhitaṃ  orena sattame divase raṭṭhaṃ me vidhamissati  ApTha Sumekhalo Kosiyo ca Siggavo cāpi Sattuko  āsādayitvā isayo duggatā te sasenakā  ApTha Yadā kuppanti isayo saññatā brahmacāriyo  sadevakaṃ vināsenti sasāgaraṃ sapabbataṃ   ApTha Tiyojanasahassamhi purise sannipātayiṃ  accayaṃ desanatthāya sayambhuṃ upasaṅkamiṃ   ApTha Allavatthā allasirā sabbe va p añjalīkatā  Buddhassa pāde nipatitvā idaṃ vacanam abravuṃ   ApTha ‘Khamassu tvaṃ mahāvīra  abhiyācati taṃ jano  pariḷāhaṃ vinodehi mā ca raṭṭhaṃ vināsāya   ApTha Sadevā manussā sabbe sadānavāsarakkhasā  ayomayena kūṭena siraṃ bhiñjeyyuṃ me sadā   ApTha Udake aggi na saṇṭhāti bījaṃ selena rūhati  agade kimi na saṇṭhāti kopo Buddhe na jāyati   ApTha Yathāpi bhūmi acalā appameyyo ca sāgaro  anantako ca ākāso evaṃ Buddho akhobhiyo   ApTha Sadā khantā mahāvīra khamitā ca tapassino  khantānaṃ khamitānañ ca gamanaṃ vo na vijjati   ApTha Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho pariḷāhaṃ vinodayi  mahājanassa purato nabhaṃ abbhuggamī tadā   ApTha  Upāli                           Tena kammen ahaṃ dhīra hīnattaṃ ajjhupāgato  samatikkamma taṃ jātiṃ pāvisiṃ abhayaṃ puraṃ   ApTha Tadāpi maṃ mahāvīra ḍayhamānaṃ susaṇṭhitaṃ pariḷāhaṃ vinodesi sayambhuñ ca khamāpayiṃ  ApTha Ajjāpi maṃ mahāvīra ḍayhamānaṃ tīh aggihi  nibbāpesi tayo aggī sītibhāvañ ca pāpayi  ApTha Yesaṃ sotāvadhān atthi suṇotha mama bhāsato  atthaṃ tuyhaṃ pavakkhāmi yathā diṭṭhapadaṃ mamaṃ  ApTha Sayambhuṃ taṃ vimānetvā santacittaṃ samāhitaṃ  tena kammen ahaṃ ajja jāto mhi nīcayoniyam   ApTha Mā vo khaṇaṃ virādhetha khaṇātītā hi socare  Sadatthe vāyameyyātha khaṇo vo paṭipādito   ApTha Ekaccāna ca vamanaṃ ekaccānañ ca virecanaṃ  visaṃ haḷāhaḷaṃ ete ekaccānañ ca osadhaṃ   ApTha Vamanaṃ paṭipannānaṃ phalaṭṭhānaṃ virecanaṃ  osadhaṃ phalalābhīnaṃ puññakkhettaṃ gavesinaṃ   ApTha Sāsanena viruddhānaṃ visaṃ haḷāhaḷaṃ yathā  āsīviso daṭṭhaviso evaṃ jhāpeti taṃ naraṃ   ApTha Sakiṃ pi taṃ haḷāhaḷaṃ uparundhati jīvitaṃ  sāsanena virujjhitvā kappakoṭim hi ḍayhati   ApTha Khantiyā avihiṃsāya mettacittavatāya ca  sadevakaṃ so tarati tasmā vo avirodhiyā  ApTha Lābhālābhe na sajjanti sammānane vimānane  paṭhavī sadisā Buddhā tasmā te n avirodhiyā  ApTha Devadatte ca vadhake core Aṅgulimālake  Dhanapāle Rāhule ca sabbesaṃ samako muni   ApTha                        ApadānaEtesaṃ paṭighaṃ n atthi rāgo mesaṃ na vijjati  sabbesaṃ samako buddho vadhakass orasassa ca   ApTha Panthe disvāna kāsāvaṃ chaḍḍitaṃ mīḷhamakkhitaṃ  sirasā añjaliṃ katvā vanditabbaṃ isiddhajaṃ   ApTha Abbhātītā ca me Buddhā vattamānā anāgatā  dhajenānena sujjhanti tasmā ete namassiyā   ApTha Satthukappaṃ suvinayaṃ dhāremi hadayen ahaṃ  namassamāno vinayaṃ viharissāmi sabbadā   ApTha Vinayo āsayaṃ mayhaṃ vinayo ṭhānacaṅkamaṃ  kappemi vinaye vāsaṃ vinayo mayhaṃ gocaro   ApTha Vinaye pāramippatto samathe cāpi kovido  Upāli taṃ mahāvīra pāde vandati satthuno   ApTha So ahaṃ vicarissāmi gāmāgāmaṃ purāpuraṃ  namassamāno sambuddhaṃ dhammassa ca sūriye  virocissati taṃ niccaṃ samantā aṭṭhayojanaṃ   ApTha Kappasatasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tusitāhi cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito  Gotamassa bhagavato atrajo so bhavissati   ApTha Sace vaseyya āgāraṃ cakkavattī bhaveyya so  aṭṭhānaṃ etaṃ yaṃ tādi agāre ratim ajjhagā   ApTha Nikkhamitvā agāramhā pabbajissati subbato  Rāhulo nāma nāmena arahā so bhavissati   ApTha Kikī va aṇḍaṃ rakkheyya camarīriva vāladhiṃ  nipako sīlasampanno mamaṃ rakkhi mahāmuni   ApTha Tassāhaṃ dhammam aññāya vihāsiṃ sāsane rato  sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo   ApTha Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ Buddhassa sāsanan ti   ApTha Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Rāhulo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthā tiRāhuḷatherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃ                 TherāpadānaPadumuttaraṃ bhagavantaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ  pabbhāramhi nisinnaṃ taṃ upagañchiṃ naruttamaṃ   ApTha Kaṇikāraṃ pupphitaṃ disvā vaṇṭaṃ chetvān ahaṃ tadā  alaṅkaritvā chattamhi Buddhassa abhiropayiṃ   ApTha Piṇḍapātañ ca pādāsiṃ paramannaṃ subhojanaṃ  Buddhena navame tattha samaṇe aṭṭha bhojayiṃ   ApTha Anumodi mahāvīro sayambhū aggapuggalo  Iminā chattadānena paramannappavecchanā  ApTha Tena cittappasādena sampattim anubhossati  tiṃsakhattun ca devindo devarajjaṃ karissati   ApTha Ekavīsatikhattuñ ca cakkavatti bhavissati  padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  ApTha Yaṃ vadanti Sumedho ti bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ kappe to satasahasse eso Buddho bhavissati   ApTha Sāsane dippamānamhi manussattaṃ gamissati  Upaseno ti nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   ApTha Carimaṃ vattate mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samūhatā  dhāremi antimam dehaṃ jetvā Māraṃ savāhanaṃ   ApTha Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ Buddhassa Padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  varanāgo mayā dinnorīsādanto urūḷhavo   ApTha Setacchattopasevito sāthabbaṇo sahatthipo  agghāpetvāna taṃ sabbaṃ saṅghārāmam akārayiṃ   ApTha Catupaññāsasahassāni pāsāde kārayim ahaṃ  mahābhattaṃ karitvāna niyyātesiṃ mahesino   ApTha Anumodi mahāvīro sayambhū aggapuggalo  sabbe jane hāsayanto deseti amataṃ padaṃ   ApTha Tam me buddho viyākāsi jaladuttamanāyako  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha ‘Catupaññāsasahassāni pāsāde kārayiṃ ahaṃ  Kathayissāmi vipākaṃ suṇotha mama bhāsato   ApTha Aṭṭhārasasahassāni kūṭāgārā bhavissare  vyamhuttamamhi nibbattā sabbasoṇṇamayā ca te   ApTha Paññāsakhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  aṭṭhapaññāsakhattuñ ca cakkavatti bhavissati   ApTha Kappasatasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito  aḍḍhe kule mahābhoge nibbattissati tāvade   ApTha So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito  Raṭṭhapālo ti nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   ApTha Padhānapahitatto so upasanto nirūpadhi  sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat anāsavo  ApTha Uṭṭhāya abhinikkhamma jahitvā bhogasampadā  kheḷapiṇḍo va bhogamhi pemaṃ mayhaṃ na vijjati   ApTha                   TherāpadānaViriyam me dhuradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādivāhanaṃ  dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane   ApTha Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḍabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ Buddhassasāsanan ti   ApTha Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Raṭṭhapālo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthā tiRaṭṭhapālatherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃabbhāraṃ sodhayantassa pavare pabbatuttame  Siddhattho nāma bhagavā āgacchi mama santikaṃ   ApTha Buddhaṃ upagataṃ disvā lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  santharaṃ paññāpetvāna pupphāsanam adās ahaṃ   ApTha Pupphāsane nisīditvā Siddhattho lokanāyako  mamañ ca gatim aññāya aniccattam udāhari   ApTha Aniccā vata saṅkhārā uppādavayadhammino  uppajjitvā nirujjhanti tesaṃ vūpasamo sukho   ApTha Idaṃ vatvāna sabbaññū lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  nabham abbhuggamī vīro haṃsarājā va ambare   ApTha Sakaṃ diṭṭhiṃ jahitvāna bhāvayāniccasaññ ahaṃ  ekāhaṃ bhāvayitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ   ApTha Dvesampattī anubhotvā sukkamūlena codito  pacchime bhave sampatte sapākaṃ yonupāgamiṃ  ApTha Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  jātiyā sattavasso haṃ arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   ApTha Āraddhaviriyo pahitatto sīlesu susamāhito  tosetvāna mahānāgaṃ alatthaṃ upasampadaṃ   ApTha  Sumaṅgala                    Catunavut ito kappe yaṃ kammam akariṃ tadā  duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Catunavut ito kappe yaṃ saññaṃ bhāvayiṃ gāthāyo abhāsitthā tiSopākatherassa apadānaṃ samattaṃĀhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmo haṃ paṭiyādetvāna bhojanaṃ  brāhmaṇe paṭimānento visāle mālake ṭhito   ApTha Ath addasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ Piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ tuvaṃ   ApTha Chavālātaṃ yathā kaṭṭhaṃ na kvaci kiccakārakaṃ n eva gāme araññe vā na hi taṃ kaṭṭhasammataṃ   ApTha Chavālātūpamo tvaṃ si gihinā nāpi paññatto  ubhato muttako ajja nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ   ApTha Siyā nu kho tava etaṃ ko pajāni hi te idaṃ saddhādhuraṃ pāhisi me kosajjabahulāya ca   ApTha Jigucchissanti taṃ viññū asucim āgāriko yathā  ākaḍḍhitvāna isayo codayissanti taṃ sadā   ApTha Taṃ viññū pavadissanti samatikkanta sāsanaṃ saṃvāsaṃ alabhanto hi kathaṃ jīvihisī tuvaṃ   ApTha                     TherāpadānaTidhappabhinnaṃ mātaṅgaṃ kuñjaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃ  balināgo upāgantvā Appamādarataṃ disvā uttamatthaṃ gavesakaṃ  Padumuttarasambuddho āgañchi mama santikaṃ   ApTha Timbarūsakavaṇṇābho appameyyo anupamo  rūpenāsadiso Buddho ākāse caṅkamī tadā   ApTha Suphullo sālarājā va caṅkamantaṃ evaṃ cintes ahan tadā  Devo nu kho ayaṃ satto udāhu manujo ayaṃ   ApTha Na me suto vā diṭṭho vā mahiyā ediso naro  api mantapadaṃ atthi ayaṃ satthā bhavissati   ApTha Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna tadā  manussā c eva devā ca Buddhathūpaṃ akaṃsu te   ApTha Mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevatā  mayam pi thūpaṃ karissāma lokanāthassa tādino   ApTha Indanīlaṃ mahānīlaṃ atho jotirasaṃ maṇiṃ nāgā ca Buddhathūpaṃ akaṃsu te   ApTha Mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevakā  mayam pi thūpaṃ karissāma lokanāthassa tādino   ApTha Sabbamaṇimayaṃ thūpaṃ akar uttarakañcukaṃ yojanan te pi vaḍḍhesuṃ āyataṃ Buddhacetiyaṃ   ApTha Catuyojanam ubbiddho Buddhathūpo virocati  obhāseti disā sabbā sataraṃsīva uggato   ApTha                     TherāpadānaYakkhā tattha samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā  manussā c eva devā ca nāgā ca garuḷā tathā   ApTha Paccekam Buddhaseṭṭhassa akaṃsu thūpam uttamaṃ  mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevakā   ApTha Mayam pi thūpaṃ karissāma lokanāthassa tādino  phaḷikā chādayissāma āyataṃ Buddhacetiyaṃ   ApTha Yojanan te pi vaḍḍhesuṃ āyataṃ Buddhacetiyaṃ  pañcayojanam ubbiddho thūpo obhāsate tadā   ApTha Gandhabbā ca samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā  manujā devatā nāgā kumbhaṇḍā guyhakā tathā   ApTha Sabbe katā Buddhathūpaṃ mayam ettha akārakā  mayam pi thūpaṃ karissāma lokanāthassa tādino   ApTha Vediyo satta katvāna yāva jaṅghā akaṃsu te  sabbasovaṇṇayaṃ thūpaṃ gandhabbā kārayuṃ tadā   ApTha Sattayojanam ubbiddho thūpo obhāsate tadā  rattindivā na ñāyanti āloko hoti sabbadā   ApTha Atihonti hi tass ābhā candasurāsatārakā  samantā yojanasate padīpo dinapajjali  ApTha Tena kālena ye keci thūpaṃ pūjenti mānusā  na te thūpam āruhanti ambare ukkhipanti te   ApTha Devehi ṭhapito yakkho Abhisammatanāmako  dhajaṃ vā pupphadāmaṃ vā abhiropeti uttari   ApTha Na te passanti taṃ yakkhaṃ dāmaṃ passanti gacchato  evaṃ passitvā gacchantā sabbe gacchanti suggatiṃ   ApTha Visaddhā ye pāvacane pasannā ye ca sāsane  pāṭihīraṃ daṭṭhukāmā thūpaṃ pūjenti mānusā   ApTha Nagare Haṃsavatiyā ahosi vadako tadā  amoditaṃ janaṃ disvā evaṃ cintes ahaṃ tadā   ApTha Uḷāro bhagavān eso yassa dhātughar edisaṃ  imā hi janatā tuṭṭhā kāraṃ kubbanti tappare  ApTha Aham pi kāraṃ karissāmi lokanāthassa tādino  tassa dhammesu dāyādo bhavissāmi anāgate   ApTha  Upavāna                   Sudhotaṃ rajakenāhaṃ uttareyyapaṭaṃ mama  veḷagge ālaggetvāna dhajam ukkhipi ambare   ApTha Abhisammatako gayha ambare hāsi me dhajaṃ  vāt eritaṃ dhajaṃ disvā bhiyyo hāsaṃ janes ahaṃ   ApTha Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā samaṇaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ  taṃ bhikkhum abhivādetvā vipākaṃ pucch ahaṃ dhaje   ApTha So me kathesi ānandaṃ pītisañjananaṃ mama  tassa dhajassa vipākaṃ anubhossasi sabbadā   ApTha Hatthī assā rathā pattī senā ca caturaṅginī  parivārenti taṃ niccaṃ dhajadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhiṃ turiyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatā  parivārenti taṃ niccaṃ dhajadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Chalāsītisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā  vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā   ApTha Aḷārapamhā hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimā  parivārenti taṃ niccaṃ dhajadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissasi  asītikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissasi   ApTha Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā cakkavattī bhavissasi  padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  ApTha Kappasatasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito  puññakammena saṃyutto brahmabandhu bhavissasi  ApTha Asītikoṭiṃ chaḍḍetvā dāse kammakare bahū  Gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissasi  ApTha Ārādhayitvā Tamandhakārā pihitā tividhaggī pi ḍayhare  etādise bhaye jāte n atthi koci vināyako   ApTha Buddho loke samuppanno dippati jinasāsanaṃ sakkā uttaritum attā puññakammena jantunā   ApTha Uggayha tīṇisaraṇe paripuṇṇāni gopayaṃ  tena kammena sukatena parimokkhāmi duggatiṃ   ApTha Nisabho nāma samaṇo Buddhassa aggasāvako  tam ahaṃ upagantvāna saraṇāgamanaṃ gahiṃ   ApTha Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade  tāvatā saraṇāgamaṇaṃ paripuṇṇam agopayiṃ   ApTha Carime vattamāṇamhi saraṇan tam anussariṃ tena kammena sukatena Tāvatiṃsaṃ agaṃch ahaṃ   ApTha Devaloke gato santo puññakammasamāhito      TherāpadānaEkaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā sire katvāna añjaliṃ  sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha Yathāṇḍajā ca saṃsedā opapātī jalābujā  kākādipakkhino sabbe antalikkhe padesagā  ApTha Ye keci pāṇabhūt atthi saññino va asaññino  sabbe te tava ñāṇamhi anto honti samogadhā  ApTha Gandhā ca pabbateyyā ye Himavante naguttame  sabbe te tava sīlamhi kalāyo pi na yujjare   ApTha Mohandhakāraṃ pakkhanto ayaṃ loko sadevako  tava ñāṇamhi jotante andhakārā vidhaṃsitā   ApTha Yathā atthaṅgate suriye honti sattā tamogatā  evaṃ buddhe anuppanne hoti loko tamogato  ApTha Yathodayanto ādicco vinodeti tamaṃ sadā  tath eva tvaṃ buddhaseṭṭha viddhaṃsesi tamaṃ sadā   ApTha Padhānaṃ pahitatto si Buddho loke sadevake  tava kammābhiraddhena tosesi janataṃ bahuṃ   ApTha Taṃ sabbaṃ anumoditvā Padumuttaro mahāmuṇi  nabhe abbhuggamī vīro haṃsarājā va ambare   ApTha Abbhuggantvāna sambuddho mahesi Padumuttaro  antalikkhe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsathā   ApTha Yen idaṃ thavitaṃ hīno va jātiyā santo Upāli nāma hessati   ApTha  Koliyavessa                 So ca pacchā pabbajitvā virājetvāna pāpakaṃ  sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat anāsavo  ApTha Tuṭṭho ca Gotamo Buddho sakakammābhiraddho ca viharāmi anāsavo   ApTha Saṃvuto pāṭimokkhamhi indriyesu ca pañcasu  dhāremi vinayaṃ sabbaṃ kevalaṃ ratanākaraṃ   ApTha Mamañ ca guṇam aññāya satthā loke anuttaro  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ   ApTha Paṭisambhidā catasso vimokhā pi ca aṭṭh ime  chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ Buddhassa sāsanan ti   ApTha Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā Upālithero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthā bhojayiṃ buddham uttamaṃ   ApTha Añjalim paggahetvāna abhivādetvā subbataṃ  dīghasālaṃ bhagavato niyyātesim ahan tadā   ApTha Mama saṅkappam aññāya satthā loke anuttaro  paṭiggahesi bhagavā anukampāya   ApTha                    TherāpadānaImassa maccukālamhi puññakammasamaṅgino  sahassayutt assa ratho upaṭṭhissati tāvade   ApTha Tena yānen ayam poso devalokaṃ gamissati  anumodissare devā sampatte ApTha Sattasattatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī bhavissati  Yasodharā samānā te sabbe pi ekanāmakā   ApTha Dve sampattī anubhotvā vinditvā puññasañcayaṃ  aṭṭhavīsatikappamhi cakkavattī bhavissati   ApTha tosayitvāna varaṃ kaññā labhissati  varaṃ laddhā ca sā kaññā putte pabbājayissati   ApTha Pabbajitvā ca te sabbe gamissanti naguttamaṃ  jātibhedabhayā sabbe bhaginīhi saṃvasissare   ApTha Ekā ca kaññā vyādhīhi bhavissati purakkhatā  mā no jāti pabhijjī ti nikhaṇissanti khattiyā   ApTha Khattiyo nīharitvāna tāya saddhiṃ vasissati  bhavissati tadā bhedo Okkākakulasambhavo   ApTha  Koliyavessa                 Tesaṃ pajā bhavissanti Koḷiyā nāma jātiyā  tattha mānusakaṃ bhogaṃ anubhossanti nappakaṃ   ApTha Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna devalokaṃ gamissati  tatrāpi pavaraṃ vyamhaṃ vindissati manoramaṃ  ApTha ApTha Uyyojitā mayā c ete nimantesuṃ Tathāgataṃ  kevalaṃ bhikkhusaṅghañ ca puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ   ApTha Sataṃ sahassaṃ pallaṅkaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ gonakatthataṃ tulikā paṭalikāya khomakappāsikehi ca        TherāpadānaVessabhussa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino  sabbe janā samāgamma mahāpūjaṃ karonti te   ApTha Sudhāya piṇḍaṃ katvāna āveḷaṃ sumanāy ahaṃ  sīhāsanassa purato abhiropes ahan tadā   ApTha Sabbe janā samāgamma pekkhanti puppham uttamaṃ  ken idaṃ pūjitaṃ pupphaṃ Buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino   ApTha Tena cittappasādena Nimmānam upapajj ahaṃ  anubhosiṃ sakaṃ kammaṃ pubbe sukatam attano   ApTha Yaṃ yaṃ yonūpapajjāmi devattam atha mānusaṃ  sabbesānaṃ piyo homi pupphapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Nābhijānāmi kāyena vācāya uda cetasā  saṃyatāna tapassīnaṃ katam uṭṭhāhitaṃ mayā   ApTha Tena ApTha  Pupphacchattiya             Siddhattho ca lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  bhikkhusaṅghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha ‘Yo me cittaṃ pasādetvā pupphacchattam akārayi  tena cittappasādena                   TherāpadānaVipassī nāma sambuddho lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  khīṇāsavehi sahito saṅghārāme vasī tadā   ApTha Ārāmadvārā nikkhamma Vipassī lokanāyako  sahasatasahassehi aṭṭha khīṇāsavehi tu  ApTha Ajinena nivattho haṃ vākaciradharo pi ca  kusumbhodakam ādāya sambuddham upasaṅkamiṃ   ApTha Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā vedajāto katañjali  kusumbhodakam ādāya Buddham abbhukkirim ahaṃ   ApTha Tena kammena sambuddho jalajuttamanāmako  mama kammaṃ pakittetvā agamā yena patthitaṃ   ApTha Phussitā pañcasahassā yehi pūjes ahaṃ jinaṃ  aḍḍhateyyasahassehi devarajjam akārayiṃ   ApTha Aḍḍhateyyasahassehi cakkavattī ahos ahaṃ  avasesena kammena arahattam apāpuṇiṃ  ApTha Devarājā yadā homi manujādhipati yathā  tam yeva nāmadheyyam me Phussito nāma hom ahaṃ   ApTha Devabhūtassa vasso tathā gandho pavāyati  sārīriko mamaṃ gandho aḍḍhakose pavāyati   ApTha Dibbagandhaṃ sampavantaṃ puññakammasamaṅginaṃ gandhaṃ ghatvāna jānanti Phussito āgato idha   ApTha  Pabhaṅkara bhagavato dhammaṃ sacchikarissati   ApTha Aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ sabbaññussa mahesino  ekāhaṃ sāṭakaṃ datvā patto mhi amataṃ padaṃ   ApTha Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā vasato suññake ghare  dhāreti pubbaṇhasamayaṃ Buddho bhavanam āgamissati   ApTha Lābhā amhaṃ suladdhaṃ no y esāma tava santike  mayam pi buddhaseṭṭhassa pūjaṃ karissāma satthuno   ApTha Annaṃ pānaṃ paṭṭhapetvā kālam arocayim ahaṃ  vasīsatasahassehi upesi lokanāyako   ApTha Sataṅgikehi turiyehi paccuggaman akās ahaṃ  sabbasovaṇṇaye pīṭhe nisīdi purisuttamo   ApTha Uparicchannam akāsiṃ sabbasovaṇṇayaṃ tadā  vījanīyā pavāyanti bhikkhusaṅghassa antare   ApTha Bahuken annapānena bhikkhusaṅgham atappayiṃ  paccekadussayugale bhikkhusaṅghass adās ahaṃ   ApTha Yaṃ vadanti Samedho ti lokāhutipaṭiggahaṃ  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha Yo me annañ ca pānañ ca saṅgham etena tappayi  tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   ApTha Aṭṭhārase kappasate devaloke ramissati  sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   ApTha Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattam atha mānusaṃ  sabbadā sabbasovaṇṇaṃ chadanaṃ dhārayissati   ApTha Tiṃsakappasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha  Ajita                   Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat anāsavo   ApTha Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā sīhanādaṃ nadissati  citake chattaṃ dhāreti heṭṭhā chattamhi ḍayhatha   ApTha Sāmaññaṃ me anuppattaṃ kilesā jhāpitā mayā  maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā santāpo me na vijjati   ApTha Tiṃsakappasahassamhi yaṃ dānam adadiṃ tadā  duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sabbadānass  ApTha Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  pathaviyaṃ sattasataṃ vipulaṃ rajjaṃ karissati  padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ  ApTha Iminā dīpadānena dibbacakkhu bhavissati     Kappasatasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissat anāsavo  ApTha Tosayitvāna ApTha Uddālakā pāṭalikā yūthikā ca piyaṅgukā  bimbijālakasañchannā samantā aḍḍhayojanaṃ   ApTha Mātaṅgā vā sattaliyo pāṭalī sindhuvāritā  aṅkolakā bahū tattha tālakuṭṭhā ca pupphitā   ApTha Sāleyyakā bahū tattha pupphitā mama assame  etesu pupphamānesu sobhanti pādapā bahū   ApTha Samantā tena gandhena vāyate mama assame  harīṭakā āmalakā ambā jambū vibhītakā   ApTha Kolā bhallāṭakā bellā phārusakaphalāni ca  tindukā ca piyālā ca madhukā kāsumāriyo  ApTha Labujā panasā tattha kadalī candarīphalā  ambāṭakā bahū tattha vallikāraphalāni ca   ApTha Viṭapā ca sapākā ca phalitā mama assame  ālakā isimuggā ca tato coraphalā bahū   ApTha Avaṭā pakkabharitā pilakkh udumbarāni ca  pipphalī maricā tattha nigrodhā ca kapitthanā   ApTha Udumbarakā bahavo kaṇḍapakkā ca pāriyo  ete c aññe ca bahavo phalino mama assame   ApTha Puppharukkhā pi bahavo pupphitā mama assame  āluvā ca kaḷambā ca biḷālitakkaḷāni ca   ApTha Ālakā tālakā c eva vijjanti mama assame  assamassāvidūre me mahājātassaro ahū  ApTha Acchodako sītajalo sūpatittho manoramo  padumupphalā bahū tattha puṇḍarīkasamāyutā  ApTha  Upasīva                  Mandālakehi sañchannā nānāgandhasameritā  gabbhaṃ gaṇhanti padumā aññe pupphanti kesarī   ApTha Opupphapattā tiṭṭhanti padumākaṇṇikā bahū  madhu bhisamhā savati khīraṃ sappi muḷālibhi  ApTha Samantā tena gandhena nānāgandhasameritā  kumudā ambagandhī ca nayitā dissare bahū   ApTha Jātassarassānukūlā ketakā pupphitā bahū  suphullā bandhujīvā ca setavārī sugandhikā   ApTha Kumbhīlā suṃsumārā ca gahakā tattha jāyare  uggāhakā ajagarā tattha jātassare bahū   ApTha Pāṭhīnā pāvusā macchā jalajā muñjarohitā  macchakacchapasañchannā atho pappaṭakehi ca   ApTha Pārevaṭā ravihaṃsā kutthakā ca nadīcarā  tiṭibhā cakkavākā ca pampakā jīvajīvakā   ApTha Kalandakā ukkusā ca senakā uddharā bahū  koṭṭhakā sukkapotā ca kuḷīrā camarā bahū   ApTha Kāreriyo ca tilakā upajīvanti taṃ saraṃ  sīhā vyagghā ca dīpī ca acchakokataracchayo   ApTha Vānarā kinnarā c eva dissanti mama assame  tāni gandhāni ghāyanto bhakkhayanto phalān ahaṃ   ApTha Gandhodakaṃ pivanto ca nivasāmi mam assame  enī migā varāhā ca pasadā khuddarūpakā   ApTha Aggikā jotikā c eva vasanti mama assame  haṃsā koñcā mayūrā ca sahitā pi ca kokilā   ApTha Mañjarikā bahū tattha kosikā poṭṭhasīsikā  pisācā dānavā c eva kumbhaṇḍā rakkhasā bahū   ApTha Garuḷā pannagā c eva vasanti mama assame  mahānubhāvā isayo santacittā samāhitā   ApTha                       TherāpadānaKamaṇḍaludharā sabbe ajinuttaravāsino  te jaṭābhārabharitā vasanti mama assame   ApTha Yugamattañ ca pekkhantā nipakā santavuttino  lābhālābhena santuṭṭhā vasanti mama assame   ApTha Vākacīraṃ dhunantā te poṭhentā ajinacammakaṃ  sabalehi upatthaddhā gacchanti ambare tadā   ApTha Na te dakam āharanti kaṭṭham vā aggidārukaṃ  ayam ca upasampanno pāṭihīrass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Lohadoṇiṃ gahetvāna vanamajjhe vasanti te  kuñjarā va mahānāgā asambhītā va kesarī   ApTha Aññe gacchanti Goyānam aññe Pubbavidehanaṃ aññe ca Uttarakuruṃ sakaṃ balam apassitā  ApTha Tato piṇḍam āharitvā paribhuñjanti ekato  sabbesaṃ pakkamantānam uggatejanatādinaṃ   ApTha Ajinacammasaddena vanaṃ sadd āyate tadā  edisā te mahāvīra sissā uggatapā mama   ApTha Parivuto ahaṃ tehi vasami mama assame  tositā sakakammena vinītāpi samāgatā   ApTha Ārādhayiṃsu mam ete sakakammābhilābhino  sīlavantā ca nipakā appamaññāsu kovidā   ApTha Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  samayaṃ saṃviditvāna upagacchi vināyako   ApTha Upagantvāna sambuddho ātāpi nipako muni  pattaṃ paggayha sambuddho bhikkhāya mam upāgami  ApTha Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ jalajuttamanāyakaṃ  tiṇattharaṃ paññāpetvā sālapuppehehi okiriṃ   ApTha Nisīditvāna sambuddho haṭṭho saṃviggamānaso  khippaṃ pabbatam āruyha agalum agahiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Kumbhamattaṃ gahetvāna vanasaṇḍe va gandhikaṃ khandhe āropayitvāna upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ   ApTha  Upasīva                  Phalaṃ Buddhassa datvāna agalum anulimp ahaṃ pasannacitto sumano buddhasettham a vandi haṃ   ApTha Paḍumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ patiggaho  isimajjhe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha Yo me phalañ cāgaluñ ca āsanañ ca adāsi me  tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   ApTha Game vā yadi vāraññe pabbhāresu guhāsu vā  imassa cittam aññāya nibbattissati bhojanaṃ   ApTha Devaloke manusse vā upapanno ayaṃ naro  bhojanehi ca vatthehi parisaṃ tappayissati   ApTha Upapajjati yaṃ yoniṃ devattam atha mānusaṃ  akkhobhabhogo hutvāna saṃsarissat ayaṃ naro   ApTha Tiṃsakappasahassāni devaloke ramissati  sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   ApTha Ekasattatikkhattuñ ca devarajjaṃ karissati  Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gananāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   ApTha Kappasatasahassamhi Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  sabbāsave pariññāya viharissat anāsavo   ApTha Suladdhalābho laddho me yo haṃ addakkhi nāyakaṃ  tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ Buddhassa sāsanaṃ   ApTha Gāme vā yadi vāraññe pabbhāresu guhāsu vā  mama saṅkappam apadānaṃ samattaṃ                         TherāpadānaMigaluddo pure āsiṃ araññe kānane ahaṃ  pasadamigaṃ gavesanto sayambhum addasam ahaṃ   ApTha Anuruddho nāma sambuddho sayambhū aparājito  vivekakāmo so vīro vanamajjh ogahiṃ tadā   ApTha Catudaṇḍe gahetvāna catuṭṭhāne ṭhapes ahaṃ  maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā padumapupphehi chādayiṃ   ApTha Maṇḍapaṃ chādayitvāna sayambhum abhivādayiṃ  dhanuṃ tatth eva nikkhippa pabbajim anagāriyaṃ   ApTha Naciraṃ pabbajitassa vyādhi me udapajjatha  pubbakammaṃ saritvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ   ApTha Pubbakammena saṃyutto Tusitam agamās ahaṃ  tattha sovaṇṇayaṃ vyamhaṃ nibbattati yadicchakaṃ   ApTha Sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ dibbaṃ yānam adhiṭṭhito  ārohitvāna taṃ yānaṃ gacchām ahaṃ yadicchakaṃ   ApTha Tato me niyyamānassa devabhūtassa me sato  samantā yojanasataṃ maṇḍapo me dhariyyati  ApTha Sayane so tuvaṭṭhāmi accantapupphasanthate  antalikkhā ca padumā vassante niccakālikaṃ   ApTha Marīcike phandamāne tappamāne ca ātape  na maṃ tapati ātapo maṇḍapassa idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Duggatiṃ samatikkanto apāyā pihitā mama  maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā santāpo me na vijjati   ApTha Mahīsaññam adhiṭṭhāya loṇatoyaṃ tarām ahaṃ  tassa me sukataṃ kammaṃ Buddhapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Apatham pi pathaṃ katvāna gacchāmi anilañjase  aho me sukataṃ kammaṃ Buddhapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha  Nanda              Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhuṃ visodhitaṃ dhammaddhajo dhammadāyādo Buddhapūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Upaṭṭhitvāna sambuddhaṃ Gotamaṃ Sakyapuṅgavaṃ  pāraṃ gamaniyaṃ maggam apucchiṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha Ajjhiṭṭho kathayī Buddho gambhīraṃ nipuṇaṃ                   TherāpadānaBodhaneyyaṃ pajaṃ disvā Piyadassī mahāmuni  cakkavālasahassamhi gantvā ovadate muni   ApTha Mam uddharitukāmo so mam assamam upāgami  na diṭṭho me jino pubbe na ssuto pi ca kassaci   ApTha Uppādā supinā mayhaṃ lakkhaṇā suppakāsitā  paṭṭho bhumm antalikkhasmiṃ nakkhattapadakovido   ApTha So haṃ Buddhassa sutvāna tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ  bhuñjanto vā nisinno vā sarāmi niccakālikaṃ   ApTha Mayi evaṃ sarantamhi bhagavā pi anussari  Buddham anussarantassa pīti me hoti tāvade   ApTha Kālañ ca punar āgamma upesi maṃ mahāmuni  sampatto pi na jānāmi ayaṃ Buddho mahāmuni   ApTha Anukampako kāruṇiko Piyadassī mahāmuni  sañjānāpesi attānaṃ ahaṃ Buddho sadevake   ApTha Sañjānitvāna sambuddhaṃ Piyadassiṃ mahāmuniṃ  sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   ApTha Aññe piṭṭhe ca pallaṅke āsandisu nisīdare  tuvaṃ si sabbadassāvī nisīda ratanāsane   ApTha Sabbaratanamayaṃ pīṭhaṃ nimminitvāna tāvade  Piyadassissa munino āsanam iddhinimmitaṃ   ApTha Ratane ca nisinnassa pīṭhake iddhinimmite  kumbhamattaṃ jambuphalam adāsi tāvade ahaṃ   ApTha Mama hāsaṃ janetvāna paribhuñji mahāmuni  tadā cittaṃ pasādetvā satthāram abhivādayiṃ   ApTha Piyadassī tu bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  ratanāsanam āsīno imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha Yo me ratanamayaṃ pīṭham amatañ ca phalam adā  tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   ApTha Sattasattatikappāni devaloke ramissati  pañcasattatikkhattuñ ca cakkavattī bhavissati   ApTha Dvattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati  padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ   ApTha  Hemaka                   Sovaṇṇayaṃ rūpimayaṃ pallaṅkaṃ sukataṃ bahuṃ  lohitaṅkamayañ c eva lacchati ratanāsanaṃ  ApTha Caṅkamantam pi manujaṃ puññakammasamaṅginaṃ  pallaṅkāni anekāni parivāressare sadā   ApTha Kūṭāgārā ca pāsādā sayanañ ca mahārahaṃ  imassa cittam aññāya nibbattissanti tāvade   ApTha Saṭṭhiṃ nāgasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanavāsasā   ApTha Ārūḷhā gāmanīyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi  imaṃ paricarissanti ratanapīṭhass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhiṃ assasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  ājāniyā va jātiyā sindhavā sīghavāhanā   ApTha Ārūḷhā gāmanīyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  te pi maṃ paricarissanti ratanapīṭhass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhiṃ rathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  dīpā atho pi veyyagghā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā   ApTha Ārūḷhā gāmaṇīyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ ratanapīṭhass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhiṃ dhenusahassāni rohaññā puṅgavūsabhā  vacchake janayissanti ratanapīṭhass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Soḷasitthisahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā   ApTha Āḷārapamhā hasuḷā susoññā tanumajjhimā  parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ ratanapīṭhass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Aṭṭhārase kappasate Gotamo nāma cakkhumā  tam ApTha Ājāniye va jātiyā sindhave sīghavāhino  ārūḷhe gāmanīyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi   ApTha Pahāyitvāna te sabbe nikkhamiṃ anagāriyaṃ  saṭṭhiṃ rathasahassāni sabbālaṅkārabhūsite   ApTha Dīpe atho pi Saṭṭhigāmasahassāni paripuṇṇāni sabbaso  chaḍḍayitvāna taṃ rajjaṃ pabbajim anagāriyaṃ   ApTha Nagarā nikkhamitvāna Himavantam upāgamiṃ  Bhāgīrasīnadītīre assamaṃ māpayim ahaṃ   ApTha Paṇṇasālaṃ karitvāna agyāgāram akās ahaṃ  āraddhaviriyo pahitatto vasāmi assame ahaṃ   ApTha Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā suññāgāre va jhāyato  na uppajjatha tāso me na passe bhayabheravaṃ   ApTha Sumedho nāma sambuddho aggo kāruṇiko muni  ñāṇālokena jotento loke uppajji tāvade   ApTha Mama assamasāmantā yakkho āsi mahiddhiko  Buddhaseṭṭhamhi uppanne ārocesi mamaṃ tadā   ApTha ‘Buddho loke samuppanno Sumedho nāma cakkhumā  tāreti janataṃ sabbaṃ tvam pi so tārayissati   ApTha Yakkhassa vacanaṃ sutvā saṃviggo āsi tāvade  Buddho Buddho ti cintento assamaṃ paṭisāmayiṃ   ApTha Aggidāruñ ca chaḍḍetvā saṃsāmetvāna santhataṃ  assamam abhivanditvā nikkhamiṃ pavanā ahaṃ   ApTha Tato candanam ādāya gāmāgāmaṃ purāpuraṃ  devadevaṃ gavesanto upagacchiṃ vināyakaṃ   ApTha Bhagavā tamhi samaye Sumedho lokanāyako  catusaccaṃ pakāsento bodheti janataṃ tadā  ApTha Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna sīse katvāna candanaṃ  sambuddham abhivādetvā imā gāthā abbāsatha   ApTha Vassike pupphamānamhi santike upavāyati  tvaṃ vīra guṇagandhena disā sabbā pavāyasi   ApTha Campake nāgavanike atimuttakakeṭake  sālesu pupphamānesu anuvātaṃ pavāyati   ApTha  Todeyya                 Tava gandhaṃ suṇitvāna Himavantā idhāgamiṃ  pūjemi taṃ mahāvīra lokajeṭṭha mahāyasa   ApTha Varacandanen ānulimpiṃ Sumedhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā tuṇhi aṭṭhāsi tāvade   ApTha Sumedho nāma bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho  bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha ‘Yo me guṇe pakittesi candanañ ca apūjayi  tam ahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato   ApTha Ādeyyavākyavacano brahmā ujupatāpavā  pañcavīsatikappāni sappabhāso bhavissati   ApTha Chavīsatikappasate devaloke ramissati  sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavattī bhavissati   ApTha Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati devaloke manusse vā saṃsaranto tuvaṃ bhave   ApTha Rūpavā guṇasampanno anupakkantadehavā  akkhobhaṃ amitaṃ dussaṃ labhissasi yadicchakaṃ   ApTha Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho jalajuttamanāyako  nabham                 TherāpadānaSusampannaṃ tadā khettaṃ dhaññaṃ me phalitam ahu  pākakāle ca sampatte evaṃ cintes ahaṃ tadā   ApTha Nacchannaṃ nappaṭirūpaṃ jānantassa guṇāguṇaṃ  yo haṃ saṅghe adatvāna
