Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragū  vivekakāmo sambuddho gacchate anilañjase  ApTha Avidūre Himavato mahājātassaro ahū  tattha me bhavanaṃ āsi puññakammena saṃyutaṃ   ApTha Bhavanā abhinikkhamma addasaṃ lokanāsanaṃ  indīvaraṃ va jalitam ādittaṃ va hutāsanaṃ   ApTha Vicinaṃ nāddasaṃ pupphaṃ pūjayissan ti nāyakaṃ  Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā avandiṃ satthuno ahaṃ   ApTha Mama sīse maṇiṃ gayha pūjayiṃ lokanāyakaṃ  imāya maṇipūjāya vipāko hotu bhaddako   ApTha Padumuttaro lokavidū āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho  antalikkhe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha   ApTha ‘So te ijjhatu saṅkappo labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ  imāya maṇipūjāya anubhohi mahāyasaṃ   ApTha Idaṃ vatvāna bhagavā jalajuttamanāmako  agamāsi Buddhaseṭṭho yattha cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ   ApTha Saṭṭhikappāni devindo devarajjam akārayiṃ  anekasatakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos ahaṃ   ApTha Pubbakammaṃ sarantassa devabhūtassa me sato  maṇi nibbattate mayhaṃ ālokakaraṇo mama   ApTha Chalāsītisahassāni nariyo me pariggahā  vicittavatthābharaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā   ApTha Aḷārapamhā hasulā susoññā tanumajjhimā  parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ maṇipūjāy idaṃ phalaṃ   ApTha Sovaṇṇamayā maṇimayā lohitaṅkamayā tathā  bhaṇḍā katākatā bhonti yadicchāya pilandhanā   ApTha Kūṭāgārā guhā rammā sayanañ ca mahārahaṃ  mama saṅkappam aññāya nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ   ApTha Lābhā tesaṃ suladdhaṃ va ye labhanti upassutiṃ  puññakkhettaṃ manussānam osadhaṃ sabbapāṇinaṃ   ApTha                           TherāpadānaMayham pi sukataṃ kammaṃ yo haṃ addakkhi nāyakaṃ  vinipātā pamutto mhi patto ca acalaṃ padaṃ   ApTha Yaṃ yaṃ yonūpapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ  samantā sattaratanā āloko hoti me sadā   ApTha Tāy eva maṇipūjāya anubhotvāna sampadā  ñāṇāloko mayā diṭṭho patto mhi acalaṃ padaṃ   ApTha Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ maṇim tāpaso  tattha me caṅkamo āsi amānussikamāpito  ApTha Jaṭābhārena bharito kamaṇḍaludharo tadā  uttamatthaṃ gavesanto pavanā abhinikkhamiṃ  ApTha Cullāsītisahassāni sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ  sakakammāni pasutā vasanti pavane tadā   ApTha Assamā abhinikkhamma akaṃ pulinacetiyaṃ nānāpupphaṃ samānetvā taṃ cetiyam apūjayiṃ   ApTha Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā assamaṃ pavisām ahaṃ  sabbe sissā samāgantvā etam atthaṃ pucchiṃsu maṃ  ApTha Puḷinena kato thūpo yaṃ tvaṃ devam namassasi  mayaṃ pi ñātum icchāma puṭṭho ācikkha ma tuvaṃ   ApTha Niddhiṭṭhā no mantapade cakkhumanto mahāyasā  te kho ahaṃ namassāmi Buddhaseṭṭhamahāyase   ApTha Kīdisā te mahāvirā sabbaññū lokanāyakā  kathaṃ vaṇṇakathaṃ sīlā kīdisā te mahāyasā   ApTha Battiṃsalakkhaṇā Buddhā cattārīsaddijāpi ca  nettā gopamukhā tesaṃ jiñjukaphalasannibhā  ApTha Gacchamānā ca te Buddhā yugamattañ ca pekkhare  na tesaṃ jānu nadati sandhisaddo na suyyati  ApTha Gacchamānā ca sugatā uddharantā va gacchare  paṭhamaṃ dakkhiṇaṃ pādaṃ Buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā   ApTha Asambhītā ca te Buddhā migarājā va kesarī  nev ukkaṃsenti attānaṃ no ca vambhenti pāṇinaṃ  ApTha Mānāvamānato muttā samā sabbesu pāṇisu  anattukkaṃsakā Buddhā Buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā   ApTha Uppajjantā ca sambuddhā ālokaṃ dassayanti te  chabbikāraṃ pakampenti kevalaṃ vasudhaṃ imaṃ   ApTha  Puḷinuppādaka                        Passanti nirayaṃ c ete nibbāti nirayo tadā  pavassati mahāmegho Buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā   ApTha Edisā te mahānāgā atulyā ca mahāyasā  vaṇṇato anatikkantā appameyyā Tathāgatā   ApTha Anumodiṃsu me vākyaṃ sabbe sissā sagāravā  tathā va paṭipajjiṃsu yathāsatti yathābalaṃ   ApTha Paṭipūjenti pulinaṃ sakakammābhilāsino  saddahantā mamaṃ vākyaṃ Buddhattaggatamānasā   ApTha Tadā cavitvā Tusitā devaputto mahāyaso  uppajji mātukucchismiṃ dasasahassī pakampatha   ApTha Assamassāvidūramhi caṅkamamhi ṭhito ahaṃ  sabbe sissā samāgantvā āgacchuṃ mama santikaṃ   ApTha ‘Usabho va mahī nadati migarājā va kuñjati  suṃsumāro va saddati kiṃ vipāko bhavissati   ApTha Yaṃ pakittemi sambuddhaṃ sikatāthūpasantike  so dāni bhagavā satthā mātukucchim upāgami   ApTha Tesaṃ dhammakathaṃ katvā kittayitvā mahāmuniṃ  uyyojetvā sake sisse pallaṅkaṃ ābhujiṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Balañ ca vata me khīṇaṃ vyādhito paramen ahaṃ  Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ   ApTha Sabbe sissā samāgantvā akaṃsu citakaṃ tadā  kalebarañ ca me gayha citakaṃ abhiropayuṃ   ApTha Citakaṃ parivāretvā sīse katvāna añjaliṃ  sokasallaparetā te vikkandiṃsu samāgatā   ApTha Tesaṃ lālappamānānaṃ agamāsiṃ citan tadā  ahaṃ ācariyo tuyhaṃ mā socittha sumedhasā      TherāpadānaSaddhādhimutto sumati mama dassanalālaso  n atthi etādiso añño yathāyaṃ bhikkhu Vakkali   ApTha Tadā haṃ Haṃsavatiyā nagare brāhmaṇatrajo  hutvā sutvā etaṃ vākyaṃ taṃ ṭhānam ApTha Yo so tayā santhavito ito sattamake hani  bhikkhusaddhāvataṃ aggo tādiso hom ahaṃ mune  ApTha Evaṃ vutte mahāvīro anāvaraṇadassano  imaṃ vākyam udīresi parisāya mahāmuni   ApTha Passath etaṃ                       Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbalokavidū muni  ito satasahassamhi kappe uppajji cakkhumā   ApTha Ovādako viññāpako tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ  desanākusalo Buddho tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   ApTha Anukampako kāruṇiko hitesi sabbapāṇinaṃ  sampatte titthiye sabbe pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi  ApTha Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi suññataṃ titthiyehi ca  vicittaṃ arahantehi vasībhūtehi tādihi   ApTha Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ uggato so mahāmuni  kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo   ApTha Vassasatasahassāni āyaṃ vijjati tāvade  tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ   ApTha Tadāhaṃ Haṃsavatiyaṃ seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso  upetvā lokapajjotaṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ   ApTha Senāsanāni bhikkhūnaṃ paññāpentaṃ sa sāvakaṃ kittayantassa vacanaṃ suṇitvā mudito ahaṃ   ApTha Adhikāraṃ sasaṅghassa katvā tassa mahesino  nipacca sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   ApTha Tadahaṃ sa mahāvīro mama kammaṃ pakittayaṃ  So yaṃ sasaṅghaṃ bhojesi sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApTha So yaṃ kamalapattakkho sīhaṃso kanakattaco  maṃ pādamūle patito patthayi ṭhānam uttamaṃ   ApTha Satasahasse ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Sāvako tassa Buddhassa Dabbo nāmena vissuto  senāsanapaññāpako aggo hessat ayaṃ tadā   ApTha Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApTha Satānaṃ tīṇikhattuñ ca devarajjam akārayiṃ  satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñ ca cakkavatti ahos ahaṃ   ApTha                           TherāpadānaPadesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ tassa kammassa vāhasā   ApTha Ekanavute ito kappe Vipassī nāma nāyako  uppajji cārunayano sabbadhammavipassako   ApTha Duṭṭhacitto upavadi sāvakaṃ tassa tādino  sabbāsavaparikkhīṇaṃ ‘suddho ti ca vijāniya  ApTha Tass eva naravīrassa sāvakānaṃ mahesinaṃ  salākaṃ paggahetvāna khīrodanam adās ahaṃ   ApTha Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  Kassapo nāma nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo   ApTha Sāsanaṃ jotayitvā so abhibhuyya kutitthiye  veneyye vinayitvā ca nibbuto so sasāvako   ApTha Sasissanibbute nāthe attham entamhi sāsane  devā kandiṃsu saṃviggā muttakesā rudammukhā   ApTha Nibbāyissati dhammakkho na passissāma subbate  na suṇissāma saddhammaṃ aho no appapuññatā   ApTha Tadāyaṃ puthavī sabbā acalā sācalācalā  sāgaro ca sasoko va vinadī karuṇaṃ giraṃ   ApTha Catuddisā dundubhiyo nādayiṃsu samānusā  samantato asaniyo patiṃsu ca bhayāvahā   ApTha Ukkā patiṃsu nabhasā dhūmaketu ca dissati  sabbathalajasattā ca raviṃsu karuṇaṃ migā   ApTha Uppāde dāruṇe disvā sāsanatthañ ca sūcakaṃ saṃviggā bhikkhavo tattha cintayimha mayaṃ tadā   ApTha Sāsanena vinā sammā jīvitena alam mayaṃ  pavisitvā mahāraññaṃ yuñjāma jinasāsane   ApTha Addasamha tadāraññe ubbiddhaṃ selam uttamaṃ  nisseniyā tam āruyha nisseniṃ pātapamhase  ApTha  Dabbamalla                             Tadā ovadi no thero Buddhuppādo sudullabho  saddhā vo sulabhā laddhā thokasesañ ca sāsanaṃ   ApTha Nipatanti khaṇātītā anante dukkhasāgare  tasmā payogo kattabbo yāvaṃ ṭhāti mune mataṃ   ApTha Arahā āsi so thero anāgāmi tadānugo  susīlā itare yuttā devalokam agamhase   ApTha Nibbuto tiṇṇasaṃsāro suddhāvāse ca ekako  ahañ ca Pukkusātī ca Sabhiyo Bāhiyo tathā   ApTha KumāraKassapo c eva tattha tatth upagāmiyaṃ saṃsārabandhanāmuttā Gotamen ānukampitā   ApTha Mallesu Kusinārāyaṃ jāto gabbhe ca me sato  mātā pitā cit ārūḷhā tato nibbattito s ahaṃ   ApTha Patito dabbapuñjamhi tato Dabbo ti vissuto  brahmaceraphalenāhaṃ vimutto sattavassiko   ApTha Khīrāsanaphalenāhaṃ pañcaṅgehi upāgato  khīṇāsavo pavādena pāpehi bahu codito  ApTha Ubho puññañ ca pāpañ ca vītivatto mhi dān ahaṃ patvāna paramaṃ santiṃ viharāmi anāsavo   ApTha Senāsanaṃ paññāpayiṃ hāsayitvāna subbate  jino tasmiṃ gune tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ Maṃ pādamūle patitaṃ ekāvattasumānasaṃ  esa pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ vicittakathikatthadaṃ  ApTha Satasahasse ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  Kumāra Kassapo nāma hessati satthu sāvako   ApTha Vicittapupphadussānaṃ ratanānañ ca vāhasā  vicittakathikānaṃ so aggataṃ pāpuṇissati   ApTha Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApTha Paribbhamaṃ bhavākāse raṅgamajjhe yathā naṭo  sākhāmigatrajo hutvā migiya kucchim okkhamiṃ  ApTha Tadā mayi kucchigate vijjhavāraṃ upaṭṭhitā  sākhena cattā me mātā nigrodham saraṇaṃ gatā   ApTha Tena sā migarājena maraṇā parimocitā  pariccajitvā saṃ pāṇaṃ mam evam ovadī tadā   ApTha Nigrodham eva seveyya na Sākham upasaṃvase  Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo yañ ce Sakhasmiṃ jīvitaṃ   ApTha Tenānusiṭṭhā migayovādena  ahañ ca mātā ca tass ovādena   ApTha  Kumārakassapa                            Āgamma rammaṃ Tusitādivāsaṃ  gato pavāsaṃ sagharaṃ yath eva   ApTha Puno Kassapavīrassa attham entamhi sāsane  āruyha selasikharaṃ yuñjitvā jinasāsanaṃ   ApTha Idāni haṃ Rājagahe jāto seṭṭhikule ahuṃ  āpannagabbhā me mātā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ   ApTha Sagabbhan taṃ viditvāna Devadattam upānayuṃ  so avoca ‘vināsetha pāpikaṃ bhikkhuniṃ imaṃ   ApTha Idāni pi munindena jinena anukampitā  sukhinī ajanī mayhaṃ mātā bhikkhunupassaye   ApTha Taṃ viditvā mahīpālo Kosalo maṃ aposayi  kumāraparihārena nāmenāhañ ca Kassapo   ApTha MahāKassapam āgamma ahaṃ Komārakassapo  vammikasādisaṃ kāyaṃ sutvā Buddhena desitaṃ Vīraṅgarūpā balino saṅgāme aparājitā  tadā kupitapaccanto amhe āha mahīpatī   ApTha Etha gantvā va paccantaṃ sodhetvā avidhībalaṃ khemaṃ me vijitaṃ katvā punarethā ti bhāsatha  ApTha Tato mayaṃ avocumha yadi deyyāsi nāyakaṃ  upaṭṭhānāya amhākaṃ sodhayissāma te tato   ApTha Tato mayaṃ laddhavarā bhumipālena pesitā  nikkhittasatthaṃ paccantaṃ katvā punar upecca taṃ   ApTha Yācitvā satth upaṭṭhānaṃ rājānaṃ lokanāyakaṃ  munivaraṃ labhitvāna yāvajīvaṃ adimha taṃ   ApTha Mahagghāni ca vatthāni paṇītāni rasāni ca  senāsanāni rammāni bhesajjāni hitāni ca   ApTha Datvā sasaṅghassa muṇe Tassa tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho paṇipacca Tathāgataṃ  lūkhacīvaradhāraggaṃ patthayiṃ ṭhānam uttamaṃ   ApTha Tadā avoca bhagavā sāvake Padumuttaro  passath etaṃ purisakaṃ kucelaṃ tanudehakaṃ   ApTha  Mogharāja                         Pītippasannavadanaṃ saddhādhanasamanvitaṃ  udaggatanujaṃ haṭṭhaṃ acalaṃ sālapiṇḍitaṃ  ApTha Eso pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ saccasenassa bhikkhuno  lūkhacīvaradhārissa tassa vaṇṇagatāsayo  ApTha Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā nipacca sirasā jinaṃ  yāvajīvaṃ subhaṃ kammaṃ karitvā jinasāsane   ApTha Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsūpago ahaṃ   ApTha Paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ bhumiḍāhakakammanā  samasahassaṃ niraye aḍayhiṃ vedanaṭṭito  ApTha Tena kammāvasesena pañcajātisatān ahaṃ  manusso kulajo hutvā tatiyākāraṇ aṅkito  ApTha Pañcajātisatān eva ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApTha Pacchime bhavasampatte ajāyiṃ khattiye kule  pituno accayenāhaṃ mahārajjasamappito   ApTha Kuṭṭharogābhibhūto haṃ na rattiyaṃ sukhaṃ labhe  mogharajjasukhaṃ yasmā mogharāja tato ahaṃ   ApTha Kāyassa dosaṃ disvāna pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  Bāvariyassa dijaggassa sissattaṃ ajjhupāgamiṃ  ApTha Mahatā parivārena upecca naranāyakaṃ  apucchiṃ nipuṇaṃ pañhaṃ vāgīsaṃ vādisūdanaṃ  ApTha Ayaṃ loko paro loko brahmaloko sadevako  diṭṭhi no nābhijānāmi Gotamassa yasassiṇo   ApTha                           TherāpadānaEvaṃ abhikkantadassāviṃ atthi mañjussarānaṃ pavaraṃ sāvakaṃ abhikittayi  ApTha Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā kāraṃ katvā mahesino  vanditvā satthuno pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   ApTha Tadā Buddho viyākāsi saṅghamajjhe vināyako kubbanti satthuno   ApTha Sattayojanikaṃ thūpaṃ sattaratanavibhūsitaṃ  kāressāma mahesissa icc evaṃ mantayanti te   ApTha Kikino Kāsirājassā tadā senāya nāyako  hutvā haṃ appamāṇassa pamāṇaṃ cetiye ApTha Samaṇā brāhmaṇā c eva namassīsu katañjalī  namo te purisājañña namo te purisuttama   ApTha Khattiyena mahādānaṃ dinnaṃ sattāhikaṃ vibho  sotukāmā phalaṃ tassa vyākarohi mahāmune   ApTha Tato avoca bhagavā suṇotha mama bhāsitaṃ  appameyyamhi Buddhamhi saṅghamhi suppatiṭṭhitā   ApTha Dakkhiṇādāya khovatthaṃ Appameyyaphalā hi sā  api ve sa mahābhogo ṭhānaṃ pattheti uttamaṃ   ApTha Lābhī pariveṇaṃ akāresi mahantam iti vissutaṃ  ApTha                           TherāpadānaNiṭṭhite ca mahādānaṃ dadaṃ khajjakasaññutaṃ navadadhim madhuṃ c eva vicinaṃ neva addasaṃ   ApTha Tadā bhattaṃ ApTha Sīhanādam asambhītaṃ nadato tassa tādino  devo naro vā brahmā vā paṭivattā na vijjati   ApTha Desento pavaraṃ dhammaṃ santārento sadevakaṃ  dhammacakkaṃ pavatteti parisāsu visārado   ApTha mahāvīraṃ sutvā taṃ dhammadesanaṃ  pītivaraṃ paṭilabhiṃ sāvakassa guṇe rato   ApTha Nimantayitvā sugataṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanandanaṃ  sattāhaṃ bhojayitvā haṃ dussehi chādayiṃ tadā   ApTha Nipacca sirasā pāde katokāso katañjalī  ekamantaṃ ṭhito haṭṭho santhaviṃ jinam uttamaṃ   ApTha Namo te vālisaddūla Namo te purisuttama  Namo te sabbalokaggā Namo te abhayaṅkara   ApTha Namo te māramathana Namo te diṭṭhisūdana  Namo te santisukhada Namo te saraṇantaga   ApTha Anāthānaṃ bhavan nātho bhītānaṃ abhayappado  vissānabhūmisantānaṃ saraṇaṃ saraṇesinaṃ   ApTha Evamādihi sambuddhaṃ santhavitvā mahāguṇaṃ  avocaṃ vādisurassa gatim pappomi bhikkhuno   ApTha Tadā avoca bhagavā anantapaṭibhānavā  Yo so Buddhaṃ apūjesi sattāhaṃ saha sāvakaṃ  ApTha Guṇañ ca me pakittesi pasanno sehi pāṇihi  eso patthayate ṭhānaṃ vādisurassa bhikkhuno   ApTha  Vaṅgīsa                             Anāgatamhi addhāne lacchate taṃ manorathaṃ  devamanussasampattiṃ anubhotvā anappakaṃ   ApTha Satasahasse ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApTha Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito  Vaṅgīso nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako   ApTha Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ  paccayehi upaṭṭhāsiṃ mettacitto Tathāgataṃ   ApTha Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tusitaṃ agamās ahaṃ   ApTha Pacchime ca bhave dāni paribbājakule ahaṃ  pacchā jāto yadā āsiṃ jātiyā sattavassiko   ApTha Sabbavedavidū jāto vādasatthavisārado  vaggussaro cittakathī paravādappamaddano   ApTha Vaṅge hi jāto Vaṅgīso vacane issaro ti vā  Vaṅgīso iti me nāmaṃ abhavi lokasammataṃ   ApTha Yadā haṃ viññutaṃ patto ṭhito paṭhamayobbane  tadā Rājagahe ramme Sāriputtam ath addasaṃ   ApTha Piṇḍāya vicarantan taṃ pattapāṇiṃ susaṃvutaṃ alolakkhiṃ mitabhāsiṃ yugamattaṃ nirikkhitaṃ  ApTha Tam disvā vimhito hutvā avocaṃ man anucchaviṃ kaṇṇikāraparicitaṃ cittaṃ gāthāpadaṃ ahaṃ   ApTha Tadā so paṇḍito vīro uttaraṃ samavoca me  virāgasahitaṃ vākyaṃ katvān uddayam uttamaṃ   ApTha Vicittapaṭibhāne hi tosito tena tādinā  nipacca sirasā pāde pabbājehīti c abraviṃ  ApTha Tato maṃ sa mahāpañño Buddhaseṭṭham upānayi  mam āha vadataṃ seṭṭho saccaṃ Vaṅgīsa kacci te   ApTha                           TherāpadānaMataṃ sīsaṃ vanacchuddhaṃ api bārasavassikaṃ  tayā vijjāvisesena sace sakkosi bhāsaya   ApTha Āmā ti me paṭiññāte tīṇi sīsāni dassayi  atho nirayadevesu upapanne avācayi  ApTha Tadā paccekabuddhassa siraṃ dassesi nāyako  tato haṃ vigatārambho pabbajjaṃ samayāci haṃ  ApTha Pabbajitvāna sugataṃ santhavāmi yahiṃ tahiṃ  tato maṃ kavyacitto ti ujjhāyanti ha bhikkhavo   ApTha Tato vīmaṃsanattham me āha Buddho vināyako  takkitānaṃ imā gāthā ṭhānaso paṭibhanti vā   ApTha Na kavyacitto haṃ vīra ṭhānaso paṭibhanti me  tana dānena Vaṅgīsa ṭhānaso santhavāhi maṃ   ApTha Tadā haṃ santhaviṃ vīraṃ gāthāhi isisattamaṃ  so ṭhānaso tadā tuṭṭho jino aggaṃ ṭhapesi maṃ   ApTha Paṭibhānena cittena aññe samatimaññ ahaṃ pesal etena saṃviggo arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   ApTha Paṭibhānavataṃ aggo añño koci na vijjati  yathāyaṃ bhikkhu Vaṅgīso evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo   ApTha Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha  sumutto saravego ca kilese jhāpayiṃ madhuraṃ dhammaṃ kāraṃ katvā va tādino   ApTha Nipacca pādamūle haṃ imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ  ‘kulappasādakānaggo yo tayā santhuto mune  tādiso hom ahaṃ vīra Buddhaseṭṭhassa sāsane   ApTha Tadā mahākāruṇiko siñcanto vāmatena maṃ  āha maṃ putta vuttiṭṭha lacchase tam manorathaṃ  kathaṃ nāma jine kāraṃ katvāna viphalo siyā   ApTha Satasahasse ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena upassayādhivatthā yā devatā sokapīḷitā  vilapantā sakaruṇaṃ tatth assūni pavattayuṃ   ApThi Sabbā bhikkhuniyo tāhi upagantvāna Gotamiṃ  nipacca sirasā pāde idaṃ vacanam abravuṃ   ApThi Tattha toyalavāsittā mayam ayye rahogatā  sācalā calitā bhūmi nāditā devadundubhi  paridevā va sūyante kim atthaṃ nūna Gotami   ApThi Tadā avoca sā sabbaṃ yathāparivitakkitaṃ  tāyo pi sabbā āhaṃsu appapuññatā   ApThi  Gotamī            Bhikkhunīnilayo suñño bhūto tāhi vinā ayaṃ pabhāte viya tārāyo na dissanti jinorasā   ApThi Nibbānaṃ Gotamī yāti satehi saha pañcahi  nadīsatehi va saha Gaṅga vilapiṃsu tā   ApThi Tāsaṃ sokapahānatthaṃ avoca madhuraṃ giram  ruditena alaṃ puttā hāsakālo yaṃ ajja vo   ApThi Pariññātaṃ mayā dukkhaṃ dukkhahetu vivajjito  nirodho me sacchikato maggo cāpi subhāvito   ApThi Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ Buddhassa sāsanaṃ  ohito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samūhatā   ApThi Yassavatthāya pabbajitā agārasmā anagāriyaṃ  so me attho anuppatto sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo   ApThi Buddho tassa ca saddhammo anūno yāva tiṭṭhati  nibbātuṃ tāva kālo me mā maṃ socatha puttikā   ApThi KoṇḍaññĀnandaNandādi tiṭṭhanti Rāhulo jino  sukhito sahito saṅgho hatadappā va titthiyā   ApThi Okkākavaṃsassa yaso ussito Māramaddano  nanu sampati kālo me nibbānatthāya puttikā   ApThi Cirappabhuti yaṃ mayhaṃ patthitaṃ ajja sijjhate  Ānandabherikālo yaṃ kim vo assūhi puttikā   ApThi Sace mayi dayā atthi yadi c atthi kataññutā  saddhammaṭṭhitiyā sabbā karotha viriyaṃ daḷhaṃ   ApThi Thīnaṃ adāsi pabbajjaṃ sambuddho yācito mayā  tasmā yathā ham uddissa tathā tam anutiṭṭhatha   ApThi Tā evam anusāsitvā bhikkhunīhi purakkhatā  upecca Buddhaṃ vanditvā imaṃ vacanam abravi   ApThi                           TherīApadānaAhaṃ Sugata te mātā tvaṃ ca dhīra pitā mama  saddhammasukhado nātha ApThi Suvaṇṇarāsisaṅkāsaṃ sarīraṃ kuru pākaṭaṃ katvā dehaṃ sudiṭṭhan te santiṃ gacchāmi nāyaka   ApThi Dvattiṃsalakkhaṇūpetaṃ sappabhālaṅkataṃ tanuṃ sañjhāghanā va bālakkaṃ mātucchaṃ dassayi jino   ApThi Phullāravindasaṅkāse tarunādiccasappabhe  cakkaṅkite pādatale pāde sā sirasā pati   ApThi Paṇamāmi narādiccaṃ ādiccakulaketunaṃ  pacchime maraṇe mayhaṃ na taṃ dakkhām aham puna  ApThi  Gotamī                      Itthiyo nāma lokagga sabbadosākarā matā  yadi koc atthi doso me khamassu karuṇākara   ApThi Itthikānañ ca pabbajjaṃ yaṃ haṃ yāciṃ punappunaṃ  tattha ce atthi doso me taṃ khamassu narāsabha   ApThi Mayā bhikkhuniyo vīra tavānuññāya sāsitā  tattha ce atthi dunnītaṃ khamassu khamādhipa  ApThi Akkhante nāma khantabbaṃ kim bhave guṇabhūsane  kim uttaran te vakkhāmi nibbānāya vajantiyā  ApThi Suddhe anūne mama bhikkhusaṅghe lokā ito nissarituṃ khamante  pabhātakāle vyasanaṃ gahānaṃ disvāna niyyāti hi candalekhā   ApThi Tadetarā bhikkhuniyo jinaggaṃ tārā va candānugatā Sumeruṃ  padakkhiṇaṃ katvā nipacca pāde ṭhitā mukhan taṃ samudikkhamānā   ApThi Na tittipubban tava dassanena cakkhun na sotaṃ tava bhāsitena  cittaṃ mamaṃ kevalam ekam eva pappuyya taṃ dhammarasena tittiṃ  ApThi Nadato parisāyan te vādidappāpabhārino  ye te dakkhinti vadanaṃ dhaññā te narapuṅgava   ApThi Dīghaṅgulī tambanakhe subhe āyatapaṇhike  ye pāde paṇamissanti te pi dhaññā raṇantaga  ApThi pabbajissāmi rūpe haṃ nibbinnā munibhāṇinā  ApThi Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna tadāha sa mahīpati  anujānāmi te bhadde pabbajjā tava sijjhatu   ApThi Pabbajitvā tadā cāhaṃ sattamāse upaṭṭhite  dīpodayañ ca TherīApadānaMahāsamudde caturo pakkhipī hatthapāṇiyaṃ  telaṃ vatthigataṃ c eva vejjo komārako yathā   ApThi Ubbattayitvā puthaviṃ pakkhipī hatthapāṇiyaṃ  cittapuññaṃ yathā nāma luñciko mārako yuvā ApThi Dhītāhaṃ Buddhaseṭṭhassa nāmen Uppalasavhayā  abhiññāsu vasī bhūtā tava sāsanakārikā   ApThi Nānāvikubbanaṃ katvā dassetvā lokanāyakaṃ  nāmagottaṃ saṃsāvetvā pāde vandāmi cakkhumā   ApThi Iddhiyā ca vasī homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā  cetopariyañāṇassa vasī homi mahāmune   ApThi Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi dibbacakkhuṃ visodhitaṃ  sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā n atthi dāni punabbhavo   ApThi Atthadhammaniruttīsu paṭibhāne tath eva ca  ñāṇaṃ me vipulaṃ suddhaṃ pabhāvena mahesino  ApThi Purimānaṃ jinaggānaṃ saṅkamante nidassitaṃ adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ tuyh atthāya mahāmuni   ApThi Yaṃ mayā pasannaṃ satthuno cittaṃ sunibaddhañ ca mānasaṃ   ApThi Mamaṃ ca cittaṃ aññāya jalajuttamanāmako  tasmiṃ khaṇe mahāvīro bhikkhuniṃ dassay iddhiyā   ApThi Iddhī anekā dassesi bhikkhunī sā visāradā Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApThi Tato cutā manussesu upapannā mahākule  pītamaṭṭhavaraṃ dussaṃ adaṃ arahato ahaṃ   ApThi Tato cut Āriṭṭhapure jātā vippakule ahaṃ  dhītā Tirīṭavacchassa Ummādantī manoharā   ApThi Tato cutā janapade kule aññatare ahaṃ  pasutā nātiphītamhi sāliṃ gopem ahan tadā   ApThi Disvā paccekasambuddhaṃ pañca Isigilīpasse gāmakamhi ajāyi haṃ  ApThi Yadā Buddhāsutamatī sutānakasakaṃ tadā  yāguṃ adāya gacchantī aṭṭhapaccekanāyake   ApThi Bhikkhāya gāmaṃ gacchante disvā putte anussariṃ  khīradhārā viniggañchi TherīApadānaTadā avoca maṃ satthā Bhadde mā bhāyi assasa  anāgatamhi addhāne lacchas etaṃ manorathaṃ   ApThi Satasahasse ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApThi Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā  Paṭācārā ti nāmena hessati satthu sāvikā   ApThi Tadā haṃ muditā hutvā yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ  mettacittā paricariṃ sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ   ApThi Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApThi Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  Kassapo nāma nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo   ApThi Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro  Kāsirājā Kikī nāma Bārāṇasīpuruttame   ApThi Tass āsiṃ tatiyā dhītā Bhikkhunī iti vissutā  dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ   ApThi Anujāni na no tāto agāre va tadā mayaṃ  vīsaṃ vassasahassāni vicarimha atanditā   ApThi Komārabrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukheṭhitā  Buddh upaṭṭhānaniratā muditā satta dhītaro   ApThi Samaṇī Samaṇaguttā Bhikkhunī Bhikkhadāyikā  Dhammā c eva Sudhammā ca sattamī Saṅghadāyikā  ApThi Ahaṃ Uppalavaṇṇā ca Khemā Bhaddā ca bhikkhunī  Kisāgotamī Dhammadinnā Visākhā hoti sattamī  ApThi Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agamhase  ApThi Pacchime ca bhave dāni jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ  Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare iddhe phīte mahādhane   ApThi Yadā ca yobbanūpetā vitakkavasagā ahaṃ  naraṃ janapadaṃ disvā tena saddhiṃ agañch ahaṃ   ApThi  Paṭācārā                          Ekaputtappasūtā haṃ dutiyo kucchiyā mamaṃ tadā haṃ mātāpitaro okkāmīti sunicchitā  ApThi Na rocesi pati mayhaṃ tadā tamhi pavāsite  ekikā niggatā gehā gantuṃ Sāvatthim uttamaṃ   ApThi Tato me sāmi āgantvā sambhāvesi pathe mamaṃ  tadā me kammajā vātā uppannā atidāruṇā   ApThi Udito ca mahāmegho pasūtisamaye mama  dabbatthāya tadā gantvā sāmi sappena mārito   ApThi Tadā vijātadukkhena anāthā kapaṇā ahaṃ  kunnadiṃ pūritaṃ disvā gacchantī sakuṇālayaṃ  ApThi Bālaṃ ādāya atariṃ pārakūle ca ekako  pāyetvā bālakaṃ puttam itaraṃ taraṇāy ahaṃ  ApThi Nivattā ukkuso hāsi taruṇaṃ vilapantakaṃ itarañ ca vahī soto sāhaṃ sokasamappitā   ApThi Sāvatthinagaraṃ gantvā assosiṃ sajane mate  tadā avocaṃ sokaṭṭā mahāsokasamappitā   ApThi Ubho puttā kālakatā panthe pati mama mato  mātā pitā ca bhātā ca ekacitamhi ḍayhare   ApThi Tadā kisā ca paṇḍū ca anāthā dīnamānasā  ito tato bhamantī haṃ addasaṃ narasārathiṃ   ApThi Tato avoca mam satthā putte mā soci assasa  attānaṃ te gavesassu kiṃ niratthaṃ vihaññasi   ApThi Na santi puttā tāṇāya na pitā na pi bandhavā  antakenādhipannassa n atthi ñātīsu tāṇatā   ApThi Taṃ sutvā munino vākyaṃ paṭhamaṃ phalaṃ ajjhagaṃ pabbajitvāna naciraṃ arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   ApThi                           TherīApadānaIddhīsu ca vasī homi dibbāya sotadhātuyā  paracittāni jānāmi satthu sāsanakārikā   ApThi Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ  aggaṃ Vinayadhārīnaṃ Paṭācārā ca ekikā   ApThi Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ Buddhassa sāsanaṃ  ohito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samūhatā   ApThi Yass atthāya jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ nānāratanapajjote mahāsukhasamappitā   ApThi  BhaddāKuṇḍalakesā                     Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ  tato jātappasādāhaṃ upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ   ApThi Tadā mahākāruṇiko Padumuttaranāyako  khippābhiññānam aggatte ṭhapesi bhikkhuniṃ subhaṃ   ApThi Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā dānaṃ datvā mahesino  nipacca sirasā pāde taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ   ApThi Anumodi mahāvīro bhadde yan te bhipatthitaṃ  samijjhissati taṃ sabbaṃ sukhinī hohi nibbutā   ApThi Satasahasse ito kappe Okkākakulasambhavo  Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati   ApThi Tassa dhammesu dāyādā orasā dhammanimmitā  Bhaddākuṇḍalakesā ti hessati satthu sāvikā   ApThi Tena kammena sukatena cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApThi Tato cutā Yāmam agaṃ tato haṃ Tusitaṃ gatā  tato ca Nimmānaratiṃ Vasavattipuran tato  ApThi Yatthayatthūpapajjāmi tassa kammassa vāhasā  tattha tatth eva rājūnaṃ mahesittaṃ akārayiṃ   ApThi Tato cutā manussesu rājūnaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ  maṇḍalīnañ ca rājūnaṃ mahesittam akārayiṃ   ApThi Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna devesu manujesu ca  sabbattha sukhitā hutvā nekakappesu saṃsariṃ   ApThi Imamhi bhaddake kappe brahmabandhu mahāyaso  Kassapo nāma nāmena uppajji vadataṃ varo   ApThi Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa tadā āsi narissaro  Kāsirājā Kikī nāma Bārāṇasīpuruttame   ApThi Tassa dhītā catutth āsiṃ Bhikkhadāyī ti vissutā  dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ   ApThi Anujāni na no tāto agāre va tadā mayaṃ  vīsaṃvassasahassāni vicarimhā atanditā   ApThi Komārabrahmacariyaṃ rājakaññā sukheṭhitā  Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā  muditā sattadhītaro   ApThi Samaṇī Samaṇaguttā ca Bhikkhunī Bhikkhadāyikā  Dhammā c eva Sudhammā ca sattamī Saṅghadāyikā   ApThi                           TherīApadānaKhemā Uppalavaṇṇā ca Paṭācārā c ahan tathā  Kisāgotamī Dhammadinnā Visākhā hoti sattamī  ApThi Tehi kammehi sukatehi cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca  jahitvā manusaṃ dehaṃ Tāvatiṃsaṃ agacch ahaṃ   ApThi Pacchime ca bhave dāni Giribbajapuruttame  jātā seṭṭhikule phīte yadā haṃ yobbane ṭhitā   ApThi Coraṃ vadhatthaṃ niyyantaṃ disvā rattā tahiṃ ahaṃ pitā me taṃ sahassena mocayitvā vadhā tato   ApThi Adāsi tassa maṃ tato viditvāna manaṃ mama  tassāhaṃ āsi vissatthā atīva dayitā hitā   ApThi So me bhūsanalobhena mālapaccāhaṭaṃ diso  corappapātaṃ netvāna pabbataṃ cetayi vadhaṃ   ApThi Tadā haṃ paṇamitvāna Sattukaṃ sukatañjalī  rakkhantī attano pāṇaṃ imaṃ vacanam abraviṃ   ApThi Idaṃ suvaṇṇakeyūraṃ muttā veḷuriyā bahū  saccaṃ harassu bhaddante mañcadāsi ti sāvaya   ApThi Oropayassu kalyāṇi mā bahuṃ paridevayi  na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi ahantvā dhanam ābhataṃ  ApThi Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato patto smi viññutaṃ  na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā   ApThi Ehi taṃ upagūhissam katvāna taṃ padakkhiṇaṃ  na ca dāni puno atthi mama tuyhañ ca saṅgamo   ApThi Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu puriso hoti paṇḍito  itthī pi paṇḍitā hoti tattha tattha vicakkhaṇā  ApThi Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu puriso hoti paṇḍito  itthī pi paṇḍitā hoti lahuṃ atthavicintikā  ApThi  BhaddāKuṇḍalakesā                     Lahuñ ca vata khippañ ca nikaṭṭhe samacetayiṃ migaṃ puṇṇāyaten eva tadā haṃ Sattukaṃ vadhiṃ  ApThi Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ na khippam anubujjhati  so haññate mandamati coro va girigabbhare   ApThi Yo ca uppattitaṃ atthaṃ khippam eva nibodhati  muccate sattusambādhā tadā haṃ Sattukā yathā   ApThi Tadā taṃ pātayitvāna giriduggamhi Sattukaṃ  santikaṃ setavatthānaṃ upetvā pabbajiṃ ahaṃ   ApThi Saṇḍāsena ca kesam me luñcitvā sabbaso tadā  pabbājetvā sasamayaṃ ācikkhiṃsu nirantaraṃ   ApThi Tato taṃ uggahetvāna nisīditvāna ekikā  samayan taṃ vicintemi suvāṇā mānusaṃ karaṃ   ApThi Chinnaṃ gayha samīpe me pātayitvā apakkami  disvā nimittaṃ alabhiṃ hatthaṃ taṃ puḷavākulaṃ  ApThi Tato uṭṭhāya samviggā apucchiṃ sahadhammike  te avocuṃ ‘vijānanti taṃ atthaṃ Sakyabhikkhavo   ApThi Sāhaṃ tam atthaṃ pucchissaṃ upetvā Buddhasāvake  te mam ādāya gañchīsu Buddhaseṭṭhassa santikaṃ   ApThi So me dhammam adesesi khandhāyatanadhātuyo  asubhāniccadukkhā ti anattā ti ca nāyako   ApThi Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvā haṃ dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ tato viññātasaddhammā pabbajjaṃ upasampadaṃ   ApThi Āyāciṃ So tadā āha ehi Bhadde ti nāyako  tadā haṃ upasampannā parittaṃ toyam addasaṃ   ApThi                           TherīApadānaPādapakkhālanenāhaṃ ñatvā saudayaṃvyayaṃ ‘tathā sabbe pi saṅkhārā iti sañcintayiṃ tadā   ApThi Tato cittaṃ vimuttam ApThi  Dhammadinnā                        Pacchime ca bhave dāni Giribbajapuruttame  jātā seṭṭhikule phīte sabbakāmasamiddhine   ApThi Yadā rūpaguṇ ūpetā paṭhame yobbane ṭhitā  tadā parakulaṃ gantvā vasiṃ sukhasamappitā   ApThi Upetvā lokasaraṇaṃ suṇitvā dhammadesanaṃ  anāgāmiphalaṃ patto sāmiko me subuddhimā  ApThi Tadā haṃ anujānetvā pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ  naciren eva kālena arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ   ApThi Tadā upāsako so maṃ upagantvā apucchatha  gambhīre nipuṇe pañhe tesabbe vyākariṃ ahaṃ   ApThi Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ  bhikkhuniṃ dhammakathikaṃ n āññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ   ApThi Dhammadinnā yathā dhīrā evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo  evāhaṃ paṇḍitā homi nāyaken ānukampitā   ApThi Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā kataṃ Buddhassa sāsanaṃ  ohito garuko bhāro bhavanetti samūhatā   ApThi Uttiṇṇavicikiccho so vītivattakathaṃkatho  sampuṇṇamanasaṅkappo patto sambodhim uttamaṃ   ApThi Anuppannassa maggassa uppādetā naruttamo  anakkhātañ ca akkhāsi asañjātam ca sañjanī  ApThi Maggaññū ca passām ahaṃ yad icchāmi dīpadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApThi Visuddhanayanā homi yasasā ca jalām ahaṃ saddhā paññā satī c eva dīpadānass idaṃ phalaṃ   ApThi Pacchime ca bhave dāni jātā vippakule ahaṃ pūjatthāya mahesissa sabbabhūtānukampino   ApThi Sattasatasahassāni puṇṇakumbhān akārayiṃ rataneh eva puṇṇāni pūjatthāya mahesino   ApThi Majjhe aṭṭh aṭṭha kumbhīnaṃ ussitā kañcanagghiyā  atirocanti   ApThi Surattaṃ sukataṃ cittaṃ cetiyaṃ ratanāmayaṃ  atirocati vaṇṇena sasañjhā va divākaro   ApThi                           TherīApadānaThūpassa medhiyo tisso haritālena pūrayiṃ  ekaṃ manosilāy ekaṃ añjanena ca ekikaṃ  ApThi Pūjaṃ etādisaṃ rammaṃ kāretvā varadhārino  adāsi dānaṃ saṅghassa yāvajīvaṃ yathābalaṃ   ApThi Sahā haṃ seṭṭhinā tena tāni puññāni sabbaso  yāvajīvaṃ karitvāna sahā va sugatiṃ ahaṃ  ApThi Sampattiyo nubhotvāna devatte atha mānuse  chāyā viya sarīrena saha ten eva saṃsariṃ   ApThi Ekanavute ito kappe Vipassī nāma nāyako  uppajji cārunayano sabbadhammavipassako  ApThi Tadā hi Bandhumatiyā brāhmaṇo sādhusammato  aḍḍho santo gamenāsi dhanena ca suduggato  ApThi Tadā hi tassāhaṃ āsiṃ brāhmaṇī samacetasā  kadāci so dijavaro saṅgamesi mahāmuniṃ   ApThi Nisinnaṃ janakāyamhi desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ  sutvā dhammaṃ pamudito adāsi sakasāṭakaṃ  ApThi Gharaṃ ekena vatthena gantvān etaṃ mam abravi  anumoda mahāpuññaṃ dinnaṃ Buddhassa sāṭakaṃ  ApThi Tadā haṃ añjaliṃ katvā anumodiṃ
